## 57:1-3 — verses 1-3 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Tafsir of Surat al-Hadid

It is Medinan.

The Imam Ahmad said: Yazid ibn Abd Rabbihi related to us, Baqiyyah ibn al-Walid related to us, Bahir ibn Sa'd related to me, from Khalid ibn Ma'dan, from Ibn Abi Bilal, from Irbad ibn Sariyah, that he told them that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to recite al-Musabbihat (the chapters beginning with glorification of Allah) before he slept, and said: "In them is a verse better than a thousand verses."

Abu Dawud, al-Tirmidhi, and al-Nasa'i related it likewise through various chains from Baqiyyah, with this content. Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan gharib (sound but singularly transmitted).

Al-Nasa'i related it from Ibn Abi al-Sarh, from Ibn Wahb, from Mu'awiyah ibn Salih, from Bahir ibn Sa'd, from Khalid ibn Ma'dan, who said: "The Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to..." and mentioned it as mursal (with a gap in the chain), not mentioning Abdullah ibn Abi Bilal nor Irbad ibn Sariyah.

The verse referred to in the hadith is, and Allah knows best, His saying: {He is the First and the Last, the Manifest and the Hidden, and He has knowledge of all things}, as will be explained, if Allah wills, and in Him is our trust.

The Almighty informs that whatever is in the heavens and the earth glorifies Him, that is, of animals and plants, as He said in another verse: {The seven heavens and the earth and whoever is in them glorify Him. And there is not a thing except that it glorifies Him in praise, but you do not understand their glorification. Indeed, He is Ever-Forbearing, Forgiving} [al-Isra: 44].

His saying: {And He is the Almighty}, that is, He to whom everything has submitted, {the Wise}, in His creation, His command, and His legislation.

{His is the dominion of the heavens and the earth. He gives life and causes death}, that is, He is the Owner who disposes of His creation as He wills, giving life and causing death, and giving whomever He wills whatever He wills, {and He is over all things competent}, that is, whatever He wills comes to be, and whatever He does not will does not come to be.

His saying: {He is the First and the Last, the Manifest and the Hidden}. This is the verse referred to in the hadith of Irbad ibn Sariyah as being better than a thousand verses.

Abu Dawud said: Abbas ibn Abd al-Azim related to us, al-Nadr ibn Muhammad related to us, Ikrimah, that is, ibn Ammar, related to us, Abu Zumayl related to us, saying: I asked Ibn Abbas, "What is this thing I find in my breast?" He said, "What is it?" I said, "By Allah, I will not speak of it." He said to me: "Is it something of doubt?" And he laughed, and said: "No one has been saved from that." He said: this continued until Allah revealed {So if you are in doubt about that which We have revealed to you, then ask those who have been reading the Scripture before you. The truth has certainly come to you from your Lord} [Yunus: 94], the verse. He said: and he said to me, "When you find something within yourself, say: {He is the First and the Last, the Manifest and the Hidden, and He has knowledge of all things}."

The expressions of the commentators on this verse have differed, and their statements amount to more than a dozen sayings.

Al-Bukhari said: Yahya said: "the Manifest over all things in knowledge, and the Hidden over all things in knowledge."

Our teacher, the Hafiz al-Mizzi, said: This Yahya is Ibn Ziyad al-Farra', who has a book he named "The Meanings of the Qur'an."

Several hadiths have come regarding this matter, among them what the Imam Ahmad said: Khalaf ibn al-Walid related to us, Ibn Ayyash related to us, from Suhayl ibn Abi Salih, from his father, from Abu Hurayrah, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to supplicate at sleep: "O Allah, Lord of the seven heavens, and Lord of the mighty Throne, our Lord and Lord of all things, Sender-down of the Torah, the Gospel, and the Furqan (the Criterion, i.e. the Qur'an), Splitter of the grain and the date-stone, there is no god but You. I seek refuge in You from the evil of everything whose forelock You hold. You are the First, there is nothing before You, and You are the Last, there is nothing after You. You are the Manifest, there is nothing above You, and You are the Hidden, there is nothing beneath You. Settle our debt on our behalf, and free us from poverty."

Muslim related it in his Sahih: Zuhayr ibn Harb related to me, Jarir related to us, from Suhayl, who said: Abu Salih used to instruct us, when one of us wanted to sleep, to lie down on his right side, then say: "O Allah, Lord of the heavens and Lord of the earth and Lord of the mighty Throne, our Lord and Lord of all things, Splitter of the grain and the date-stone, and Sender-down of the Torah, the Gospel, and the Furqan, I seek refuge in You from the evil of every possessor of evil whose forelock You hold. O Allah, You are the First, so there is nothing before You, and You are the Last, so there is nothing after You, and You are the Manifest, so there is nothing above You, and You are the Hidden, so there is nothing beneath You. Settle our debt on our behalf, and free us from poverty."

And he used to relate this from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ.

The Hafiz Abu Ya'la al-Mawsili related in his Musnad from A'ishah, Mother of the Believers, something similar to this, saying: Uqbah related to us, Yunus related to us, al-Sariyy ibn Isma'il related to us, from al-Sha'bi, from Masruq, from A'ishah, that she said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to order his bedding, and it would be spread for him facing the qiblah, and when he settled into it, he would rest his head on his right palm, then whisper, it was not known what he said, and when it was the last part of the night he would raise his voice and say: "O Allah, Lord of the seven heavens and Lord of the mighty Throne, God of all things, and Lord of all things, and Sender-down of the Torah, the Gospel, and the Furqan, Splitter of the grain and the date-stone, I seek refuge in You from the evil of everything whose forelock You hold. O Allah, You are the First, before whom there is nothing, and You are the Last, after whom there is nothing, and You are the Manifest, so there is nothing above You, and You are the Hidden, so there is nothing beneath You. Settle our debt on our behalf, and free us from poverty."

This al-Sariyy ibn Isma'il is the cousin of al-Sha'bi, and he is very weak. And Allah knows best.

Abu Isa al-Tirmidhi said, in the commentary on this verse: Abd ibn Humayd and others related to us, the meaning being the same, saying: Yunus ibn Muhammad related to us, Shayban ibn Abd al-Rahman related to us, from Qatadah, who said: al-Hasan related, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: While the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was sitting with his companions, a cloud came over them, and the Prophet of Allah ﷺ said: "Do you know what this is?" They said, "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said: "This is the anan (rain cloud), these are the water-bearers of the earth. He drives it to a people who neither thank Him for it nor call upon Him." Then he said: "Do you know what is above you?" They said, "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said: "It is the raqi' (firmament), a protected roof and a restrained wave." Then he said: "Do you know how far it is between you and it?" They said, "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said: "Between you and it is a distance of five hundred years." Then he said: "Do you know what is above that?" They said, "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said: "Above that is a heaven, the distance between them being a journey of five hundred years," until he counted seven heavens, "between every two heavens being as the distance between heaven and earth." Then he said: "Do you know what is above that?" They said, "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said: "Above that is the Throne, and the distance between it and the heaven is like the distance between the two heavens." Then he said: "Do you know what is beneath you?" They said, "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said: "It is the earth." Then he said: "Do you know what is beneath that?" They said, "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said: "Beneath it is another earth, the distance between them being a journey of five hundred years," until he counted seven earths, "between every two earths being a journey of five hundred years." Then he said: "By the One in whose hand is the soul of Muhammad, if you were to lower a rope down to the lowest earth, it would descend upon Allah." Then he recited: {He is the First and the Last, the Manifest and the Hidden, and He has knowledge of all things}.

Then al-Tirmidhi said: This is a gharib hadith from this route, and it is related from Ayyub, Yunus, that is, Ibn Ubayd, and Ali ibn Zayd, who said: al-Hasan did not hear from Abu Hurayrah. Some of the people of knowledge have explained this hadith, saying: it descended only upon the knowledge, power, and authority of Allah, and the knowledge, power, and authority of Allah are in every place, while He is upon the Throne, as He has described in His Book. His words end there.

The Imam Ahmad related this hadith from Surayj, from al-Hakam ibn Abd al-Malik, from Qatadah, from al-Hasan, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, mentioning it, and in his version the distance between the earths is a journey of seven hundred years, and he said: "If one of you were lowered by a rope to the seventh lowest earth, he would descend upon Allah," then he recited: {He is the First and the Last, the Manifest and the Hidden, and He has knowledge of all things}.

Ibn Abi Hatim and al-Bazzar related it from the hadith of Abu Ja'far al-Razi, from Qatadah, from al-Hasan, from Abu Hurayrah, mentioning the hadith, but Ibn Abi Hatim did not mention its ending, that is, his saying "if you were lowered by a rope," but only said: "until he counted seven earths, between every two earths a journey of five hundred years," then he recited {He is the First and the Last, the Manifest and the Hidden, and He has knowledge of all things}.

Al-Bazzar said: No one related it from the Prophet ﷺ except Abu Hurayrah.

Ibn Jarir related it from Bishr, from Yazid, from Sa'id, from Qatadah on {He is the First and the Last, the Manifest and the Hidden}: it was mentioned to us that the Prophet of Allah ﷺ, while sitting among his companions, a cloud rose over them, and he said: "Do you know what this is?" and he mentioned the hadith exactly as in al-Tirmidhi's account, except that it is mursal (with a gap) from this route, and this is perhaps what is preserved, and Allah knows best. It has also been related from the hadith of Abu Dharr al-Ghifari, may Allah be pleased with him and he with Allah, related by al-Bazzar in his Musnad and al-Bayhaqi in the Book of Names and Attributes, but there is doubt regarding its chain of transmission, and its text contains strangeness and objectionable elements, and Allah, glorified and exalted, knows best.

Ibn Jarir said, regarding His saying {And of the earth, the like thereof} [al-Talaq: 12]: Ibn Abd al-A'la related to us, Ibn Thawr related to us, from Ma'mar, from Qatadah, who said: Four angels met between heaven and earth, and they said to one another, "From where have you come?" One of them said, "My Lord, mighty and majestic, sent me from the seventh heaven, and I left Him there." Another said, "My Lord, mighty and majestic, sent me from the seventh earth, and I left Him there." Another said, "My Lord sent me from the east, and I left Him there." Another said, "My Lord sent me from the west, and I left Him there."

This hadith is very gharib (singularly transmitted), and it may be that the first hadith is mawquf (a halted report) attributed to Qatadah, as it is related here as his own statement, and Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

تَفْسِيرُ سُورَةِ الْحَدِيدِ

وَهِيَ مَدَنِيَّةٌ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ رَبِّهِ، حَدَّثَنَا بَقِيَّة بْنُ الْوَلِيدِ، حَدَّثَنِي بَحِيرُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ خَالِدِ بْنِ مَعْدَان، عن بن أَبِي بِلَالٍ، عَنْ عِرْبَاض بْنِ سَارِيَةَ، أَنَّهُ حَدَّثَهُمْ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ يَقْرَأُ الْمُسَبِّحَاتِ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَرْقُدَ، وَقَالَ: "إِنَّ فِيهِنَّ آيَةً أَفْضَلُ مِنْ أَلْفِ آيَةٍ".

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، مِنْ طُرُقٍ عَنْ بَقِيَّةَ، بِهِ وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ.

وَرَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي السَّرْحِ، عَنِ ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، عَنْ مُعَاوِيَةَ بْنِ صَالِحٍ، عَنْ بَحِيرُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ خَالِدِ بْنِ مَعْدَانَ قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ ... فَذَكَرُهُ مُرْسَلا لَمْ يَذْكُرْ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ أَبِي بِلَالٍ، وَلَا الْعِرْبَاضَ بْنَ سَارِيَةَ 

وَالْآيَةُ الْمُشَارُ إِلَيْهَا فِي الْحَدِيثِ هِيَ-وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ-قَوْلُهُ: ﴿هُوَ الأوَّلُ وَالآخِرُ وَالظَّاهِرُ وَالْبَاطِنُ وَهُوَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ﴾ كَمَا سَيَأْتِي بَيَانُهُ إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ وَبِهِ الثِّقَةُ 

* *

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ يُسَبِّحُ لَهُ مَا في السموات وَالْأَرْضِ أَيْ: مِنَ الْحَيَوَانَاتِ وَالنَّبَاتَاتِ، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿تُسَبِّحُ لَهُ السَّمَاوَاتُ السَّبْعُ وَالأرْضُ وَمَنْ فِيهِنَّ وَإِنْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ إِلا يُسَبِّحُ بِحَمْدِهِ وَلَكِنْ لَا تَفْقَهُونَ تَسْبِيحَهُمْ إِنَّهُ كَانَ حَلِيمًا غَفُورًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٤٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَهُوَ الْعَزِيزُ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِي قَدْ خَضَعَ لَهُ كُلُّ شَيْءٍ ﴿الْحَكِيمُ﴾ فِي خَلْقِهِ وَأَمْرِهِ وَشَرْعِهِ

﴿لَهُ مُلْكُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ يُحْيِي وَيُمِيتُ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ الْمَالِكُ الْمُتَصَرِّفُ فِي خَلْقِهِ فَيُحْيِي وَيُمِيتُ، وَيُعْطِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ مَا يَشَاءُ، ﴿وَهُوَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ﴾ أَيْ: مَا شَاءَ كَانَ وَمَا لَمْ يَشَأْ لَمْ يَكُنْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿هُوَ الأوَّلُ وَالآخِرُ وَالظَّاهِرُ وَالْبَاطِنُ﴾ وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ هِيَ الْمُشَارُ إِلَيْهَا فِي حَدِيثِ الْعِرْبَاضِ بْنِ سَارِيَةَ: أَنَّهَا أَفْضَلُ من ألف آية.

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ حَدَّثَنَا عَبَّاسُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْعَظِيمِ حَدَّثَنَا النَّضْرُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عِكْرِمَةُ-يَعْنِي بْنَ عَمَّارٍ-حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو زُمَيْل قَالَ: سألت بن عَبَّاسٍ فَقُلْتُ: مَا شَيْءٌ أَجِدُهُ فِي صَدْرِي؟ قَالَ مَا هُوَ؟ قُلْتُ وَاللَّهِ لَا أَتَكَلَّمُ بِهِ قَالَ: فَقَالَ لِي أَشَيْءٌ مِنْ شَكٍّ؟ قَالَ -وَضَحِكَ -قَالَ: مَا نَجَا مِنْ ذَلِكَ أَحَدٌ قَالَ حَتَّى أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ ﴿فَإِنْ كُنْتَ فِي شَكٍّ مِمَّا أَنزلْنَا إِلَيْكَ فَاسْأَلِ الَّذِينَ يَقْرَءُونَ الْكِتَابَ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ [لَقَدْ جَاءَكَ الْحَقُّ مِنْ رَبِّكَ] ﴾ الْآيَةَ [يُونُسَ:٩٤] قَالَ: وَقَالَ لِي: إِذَا وَجَدْتَ فِي نَفْسِكَ شَيْئًا فَقُلْ: ﴿هُوَ الأوَّلُ وَالآخِرُ وَالظَّاهِرُ وَالْبَاطِنُ وَهُوَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ﴾ 

وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفَتْ عِبَارَاتُ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ وَأَقْوَالُهُمْ عَلَى نَحْوٍ مِنْ بِضْعَةَ عَشَرَ قَوْلًا.

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: قَالَ يَحْيَى: الظَّاهِرُ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ عِلْمًا وَالْبَاطِنُ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ عِلْمًا 

قَالَ شَيْخُنَا الْحَافِظُ الْمِزِّيُّ: يَحْيَى هَذَا هُوَ بْنُ زِيَادٍ الْفَرَّاءُ، لَهُ كِتَابٌ سَمَّاهُ: "مَعَانِي الْقُرْآنِ".

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي ذَلِكَ أَحَادِيثُ، فَمِنْ ذَلِكَ مَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا خَلَفُ بْنُ الْوَلِيدِ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنْ سُهيل بْنِ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ يَدْعُو عِنْدَ النَّوْمِ: "اللَّهُمَّ، رب السموات السَّبْعِ، وَرَبَّ الْعَرْشِ الْعَظِيمِ، رَبَّنَا وَرَبَّ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، مُنْزِلَ التَّوْرَاةِ وَالْإِنْجِيلِ وَالْفُرْقَانِ، فَالِقَ الْحَبِّ وَالنَّوَى، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا أَنْتَ، أَعُوذُ بِكَ مِنْ شَرِّ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ أَنْتَ آخِذٌ بِنَاصِيَتِهِ، أَنْتَ الْأَوَّلُ لَيْسَ قَبْلَكَ شَيْءٌ وَأَنْتَ الْآخِرُ لَيْسَ بَعْدَكَ شَيْءٌ، وَأَنْتَ الظَّاهِرُ لَيْسَ فَوْقَكَ شَيْءٌ وَأَنْتَ الْبَاطِنُ لَيْسَ دُونَكَ شَيْءٌ. اقْضِ عَنَّا الدَّيْنَ، وَأَغْنِنَا مِنَ الْفَقْرِ" 

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ: حَدَّثَنِي زُهَيْرُ بْنُ حَرْبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرٌ عَنْ سُهَيل قَالَ: كَانَ أَبُو صَالِحٍ يَأْمُرُنَا إِذَا أَرَادَ أَحَدُنَا أَنْ يَنَامَ: أَنْ يَضْطَجِعَ عَلَى شِقِّهِ الْأَيْمَنِ، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: اللَّهُمَّ، ربّ السموات وَرَبَّ الْأَرْضِ وَرَبَّ الْعَرْشِ الْعَظِيمِ، رَبَّنَا وَرَبَّ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، فَالِقَ الْحَبِّ وَالنَّوَى، وَمُنْزِلَ التَّوْرَاةِ وَالْإِنْجِيلِ وَالْفُرْقَانِ، أَعُوذُ بِكَ مِنْ شَرِّ كُلِّ ذِي شَرٍّ أَنْتَ آخِذٌ بِنَاصِيَتِهِ، اللَّهُمَّ، أَنْتَ الْأَوَّلُ فَلَيْسَ قَبْلَكَ شَيْءٌ، وَأَنْتَ الْآخِرُ فَلَيْسَ بَعْدَكَ شَيْءٌ، وَأَنْتَ الظَّاهِرُ فَلَيْسَ فَوْقَكَ شَيْءٌ، وَأَنْتَ الْبَاطِنُ فَلَيْسَ دُونَكَ شَيْءٌ، اقْضِ عَنَّا الدَّيْنَ، وَأَغْنِنَا مِنَ الْفَقْرِ.

وَكَانَ يَرْوِي ذَلِكَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ 

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى الْمَوْصِلِيُّ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ عَنْ عَائِشَةَ أُمِّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ نَحْوَ هَذَا، فَقَالَ حَدَّثَنَا عُقْبَةُ، حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ، حَدَّثَنَا السَّرِيُّ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ، عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ أَنَّهَا قَالَتْ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَأْمُرُ بِفِرَاشِهِ فَيُفْرَشُ لَهُ مُسْتَقْبِلَ الْقِبْلَةِ، فَإِذَا أَوَى إِلَيْهِ تَوَسَّدَ كَفَّهُ الْيُمْنَى، ثُمَّ هَمَسَ-مَا يُدْرَى مَا يَقُولُ-فَإِذَا كَانَ فِي آخِرِ اللَّيْلِ رفع صوته فقال: "اللهم، رب السموات السَّبْعِ وَرَبَّ الْعَرْشِ الْعَظِيمِ، إِلَهَ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، وَرَبَّ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، وَمُنْزِلَ التَّوْرَاةِ وَالْإِنْجِيلِ وَالْفُرْقَانِ، فَالِقَ الْحَبِّ وَالنَّوَى، أَعُوذُ بِكَ مِنْ شَرِّ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ أَنْتَ آخِذٌ بِنَاصِيَتِهِ اللَّهُمَّ، أَنْتَ الْأَوَّلُ الَّذِي لَيْسَ قَبْلَكَ شَيْءٌ، وَأَنْتَ الْآخِرُ الَّذِي لَيْسَ بَعْدَكَ شَيْءٌ، وَأَنْتَ الظَّاهِرُ فَلَيْسَ فَوْقَكَ شَيْءٌ، وَأَنْتَ الْبَاطِنُ فَلَيْسَ دُونَكَ شَيْءٌ، اقْضِ عَنَّا الدَّيْنَ، وَأَغْنِنَا مِنَ الْفَقْرِ" 

السَّرِيُّ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ هَذَا ابْنُ عَمِّ الشَّعْبِيِّ، وَهُوَ ضَعِيفٌ جِدًّا وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو عِيسَى التِّرْمِذِيُّ عِنْدَ تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: حَدَّثَنَا عبدُ بْنُ حُمَيْدٍ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ-الْمَعْنَى وَاحِدٌ-قَالُوا: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شَيْبَانُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ عَنْ قَتَادَةَ قَالَ: حَدَّثَ الْحَسَنُ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: بَيْنَمَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ جَالِسٌ وَأَصْحَابُهُ، إِذْ أَتَى عَلَيْهِمْ سَحَاب فَقَالَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ مَا هَذَا؟ ". قَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: "هَذَا العَنَان، هَذِهِ رَوَايا الْأَرْضِ تَسُوقُهُ إِلَى قَوْمٍ لَا يَشْكُرُونَهُ وَلَا يَدْعُونه". ثُمَّ قَالَ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ مَا فَوْقَكُمْ؟ قَالُوا اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ قَالَ " فَإِنَّهَا الرَّقِيعُ، سَقْفٌ مَحْفُوظٌ، وَمَوْجٌ مَكْفُوفٌ". ثُمَّ قَالَ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ كَمْ بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَهَا" قَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: "بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَهَا خَمْسُمِائَةِ سَنَةٍ". ثُمَّ قَالَ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ مَا فَوْقَ ذَلِكَ؟ " قَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ قَالَ: " فَإِنَّ فَوْقَ ذَلِكَ سَمَاءٌ بُعدُ مَا بَيْنَهُمَا مَسِيرَةُ خمسمائة سنة-حتى عدَّ سبع سموات-مَا بَيْنَ كُلِّ سَمَاءَيْنِ كَمَا بَيْنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ". ثُمَّ قَالَ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ مَا فَوْقَ ذَلِكَ؟ " قَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: " فَإِنَّ فَوْقَ ذَلِكَ الْعَرْشَ، وَبَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَ السَّمَاءِ بُعدُ مَا بَيْنَ السَّمَاءَيْنِ". ثُمَّ قَالَ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ مَا الَّذِي تَحْتَكُمْ؟ ". قَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: "فَإِنَّهَا الْأَرْضُ". ثُمَّ قَالَ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ مَا الَّذِي تَحْتَ ذَلِكَ؟ ". قَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: "فَإِنَّ تَحْتَهَا أَرْضًا أُخْرَى بَيْنَهُمَا مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسِمِائَةِ سَنَةٍ-حَتَّى عدَّ سَبْعَ أَرَضِينَ-بَيْنَ كُلِّ أَرْضَيْن مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسِمِائَةِ سَنَةٍ". ثُمَّ قَالَ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسُ مُحَمَّدٍ بِيَدِهِ، لَوْ أَنَّكُمْ دَليتم بِحَبْلٍ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ السُّفْلَى لَهَبَطَ عَلَى اللَّهِ"، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿هُوَ الأوَّلُ وَالآخِرُ وَالظَّاهِرُ وَالْبَاطِنُ وَهُوَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ﴾

ثُمَّ قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ، ويُروى عَنْ أَيُّوبَ وَيُونُسَ-يَعْنِي بْنَ عُبَيْدٍ-وَعَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ قَالُوا: لَمْ يَسْمَعِ الْحَسَنُ مِنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ. وَفَسَّرَ بَعْضُ أَهْلِ الْعِلْمِ هَذَا الْحَدِيثَ فَقَالُوا: إِنَّمَا هَبَط عَلَى علْم اللَّهِ وَقُدْرَتِهِ وَسُلْطَانِهِ، وَعِلْمُ اللَّهِ وَقَدْرَتُهُ وَسُلْطَانُهُ فِي كُلِّ مَكَانٍ، وَهُوَ عَلَى الْعَرْشِ، كَمَا وَصَفَ فِي كِتَابِهِ. انْتَهَى كَلَامُهُ 

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ هَذَا الْحَدِيثَ عَنْ سُرَيْجٍ، عَنِ الْحَكَمُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَذَكَرَهُ، وَعِنْدَهُ بُعدُ مَا بَيْنَ الأرْضين مَسِيرَةُ سَبْعِمِائَةِ عَامٍ، وَقَالَ: "لَوْ دَلَّيْتُمْ أَحَدَكُمْ بِحَبْلٍ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ السُّفْلَى السَّابِعَةِ لَهَبَطَ عَلَى اللَّهِ"، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿هُوَ الأوَّلُ وَالآخِرُ وَالظَّاهِرُ وَالْبَاطِنُ وَهُوَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ﴾

وَرَوَاهُ بْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ وَالْبَزَّارُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي جَعْفَرٍ الرَّازِيِّ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ ... فَذَكَرَ الْحَدِيثَ، وَلَمْ يَذْكُرِ بن أَبِي حَاتِمٍ آخِرَهُ وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ: "لَوْ دَلَّيْتُمْ بِحَبْلٍ"، وَإِنَّمَا قَالَ: "حَتَّى عَدّ سَبْعَ أَرَضِينَ بَيْنَ كُلِّ أَرْضَيْنِ مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسِمِائَةِ عَامٍ"، ثُمَّ تَلَا ﴿هُوَ الأوَّلُ وَالآخِرُ وَالظَّاهِرُ وَالْبَاطِنُ وَهُوَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ﴾

وَقَالَ الْبَزَّارُ: لَمْ يَرْوِهِ عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ إِلَّا أبو هريرة.

ورواه بن جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ بِشْرٍ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ، عَنْ سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ: ﴿هُوَ الأوَّلُ وَالآخِرُ وَالظَّاهِرُ وَالْبَاطِنُ﴾ ذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْنَمَا هُوَ جَالِسٌ فِي أَصْحَابِهِ إِذْ ثَارَ عَلَيْهِمْ سَحَابٌ، فَقَالَ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ مَا هَذَا؟ " وَذَكَرَ الْحَدِيثَ مِثْلَ سِيَاقِ التِّرْمِذِيِّ سَوَاءً، إِلَّا أَنَّهُ مُرْسَلٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ، وَلَعَلَّ هَذَا هُوَ الْمَحْفُوظُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. وَقَدْ رُوِيَ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي ذَرٍ الْغِفَارِيِّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ وَأَرْضَاهُ، رَوَاهُ الْبَزَّارُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ، وَالْبَيْهَقِيُّ فِي كِتَابِ الْأَسْمَاءِ وَالصِّفَاتِ وَلَكِنْ فِي إِسْنَادِهِ نَظَرٌ، وَفِي مَتْنِهِ غَرَابَةٌ وَنَكَارَةٌ، وَاللَّهُ سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عِنْدَ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى ﴿وَمِنَ الأرْضِ مِثْلَهُنَّ﴾ [الطَّلَاقِ "١٢"] حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عَبْدِ الْأَعْلَى، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ ثَوْرٍ، عَنْ مَعْمَر، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ قَالَ: الْتَقَى أَرْبَعَةٌ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ بَيْنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ، فَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ: مِنْ أَيْنَ جِئْتَ؟ قَالَ أَحَدُهُمْ: أَرْسَلَنِي رَبِّي، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، مِنَ السَّمَاءِ السَّابِعَةِ وَتَرَكْتُهُ ثَمّ، قَالَ الْآخَرُ: أَرْسَلَنِي رَبِّي، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ السَّابِعَةِ وَتَرَكْتُهُ ثَمّ، قَالَ الْآخَرُ: أَرْسَلَنِي رَبِّي مِنَ الْمَشْرِقِ وَتَرَكْتُهُ ثَمّ، قَالَ الْآخَرُ: أَرْسَلَنِي رَبِّي مِنَ الْمَغْرِبِ وَتَرَكْتُهُ ثَمّ 

وَهَذَا [حَدِيثٌ] غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا، وَقَدْ يَكُونُ الْحَدِيثُ الْأَوَّلُ موقوفًا على قتادة كما روي هاهنا من قوله، والله أعلم.

---

## 57:4-6 — verses 4-6 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted, informs of His creating the heavens and the earth and what is between them in six days, then He informs of His rising over the Throne after creating them. The discussion of this verse and its likes has already passed in surat al-A'raf, in a manner that makes repeating it here unnecessary.

{He knows what enters into the earth} that is, He knows the number of what enters into it of seeds and rain, {and what comes out of it} of crops, plants, and fruits, as He said: {And with Him are the keys of the unseen, none knows them but He. And He knows what is in the land and the sea. Not a leaf falls but that He knows it, nor is there a grain in the darknesses of the earth, nor anything moist or dry, but that it is in a clear register} [al-An'am: 59].

His saying: {and what descends from the sky} that is, of rains, snows, and hail, and of decrees and judgments brought down together with the noble angels. It has already passed in surat al-Baqarah that no drop descends from the sky except that an angel accompanies it, setting it down in the place that Allah commands, wherever He, exalted, wills.

His saying: {and what ascends into it} that is, of angels and deeds, as has come in the sound hadith: "The deed of the night is raised up to Him before the deed of the day, and the deed of the day before the deed of the night."

His saying: {And He is with you wherever you are, and Allah is Seeing of what you do} that is, He is watchful over you, a witness over your deeds wherever you are and wherever you may be, on land or sea, by night or day, in houses or in open wastelands. All of it is equal in His knowledge, under His sight and His hearing. He hears your speech and sees your place, and He knows your secret and your private conversation, as He said: {Unquestionably, they turn away their breasts to hide themselves from Him. Unquestionably, when they cover themselves with their garments, He knows what they conceal and what they declare. Indeed, He is Knowing of that within the breasts} [Hud: 5]. And He said: {It is the same [to Him] concerning you, whether one conceals his speech or one declares it openly, and whether he is hidden by night or moves about in the day} [al-Ra'd: 10]. So there is no god besides Him and no lord other than Him. It has been established in the sound hadith that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to Jibril (peace be upon him), when he asked him about ihsan (excellence in worship): "That you worship Allah as though you see Him, and if you do not see Him, then indeed He sees you."

Al-Hafiz Abu Bakr al-Isma'ili narrated from the hadith of Nasr ibn Khuzaymah ibn Junadah ibn Mahfuz ibn Alqamah: [chain] Abd al-Rahman ibn A'idh said: Umar said: A man came to the Prophet ﷺ and said, "Give me a provision of words to live by." He said: "Feel shame before Allah as you would feel shame before a righteous man of your kinsfolk who does not leave your side."

This is a hadith gharib (singular narration). Abu Nu'aym narrated from the hadith of Abd Allah ibn Mu'awiyah al-Ghadiri, as a marfu' (elevated) report: "Three things, whoever does them has tasted faith: whoever worships Allah alone, and gives the zakat of his wealth willingly, each year, not giving the old, worn-out animal, nor the diseased one, nor the mean and inferior one, nor the sick one, but rather from the middling of your wealth, and purifies himself." A man said, "O Messenger of Allah, what is a man's purification of himself?" He said: "That he knows that Allah is with him wherever he is."

Nu'aym ibn Hammad, may Allah have mercy on him, said: [chain] Ubadah ibn al-Samit said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The most excellent of faith is that you know that Allah is with you wherever you are." Gharib (singular narration). And Imam Ahmad used to recite these two lines of poetry:

"If ever you are alone one day, do not say: I am alone, but say: over me is a watcher.

And do not ever suppose that Allah is heedless for a moment, nor that what is hidden from Him is absent."

His saying: {To Him belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth, and to Allah all matters are returned} that is, He is the Owner of this world and the next, as He said: {And indeed, to Us belongs the Hereafter and the first [life]} [al-Layl: 13]. And He is the Praised One for that, as He said: {And He is Allah, there is no god but He. To Him belongs all praise in the first [life] and the Hereafter} [al-Qasas: 70]. And He said: {Praise be to Allah, to whom belongs whatever is in the heavens and whatever is in the earth, and to Him belongs praise in the Hereafter, and He is the Wise, the Aware} [Saba: 1]. So all that is in the heavens and the earth is His possession, and their inhabitants are servants, enslaved and humbled before Him, as He said: {There is none in the heavens and earth but that he comes to the Most Merciful as a servant. He has enumerated them and counted them a [full] counting, and each of them is coming to Him on the Day of Resurrection alone} [Maryam: 93-95]. For this reason He said: {and to Allah all matters are returned} that is, to Him is the return on the Day of Resurrection, and He judges among His creation as He wills. He is the Just One who does not oppress, nor does He wrong [anyone] by so much as the weight of a speck of dust. Rather, if one of them does a single good deed, He multiplies it up to tenfold, {and gives from Himself a great reward} [al-Nisa: 40]. And as He, exalted, said: {And We place the scales of justice for the Day of Resurrection, so no soul will be wronged at all. And if there is [even] the weight of a mustard seed, We will bring it forth. And sufficient are We as accountant} [al-Anbiya: 47].

His saying: {He causes the night to enter into the day and causes the day to enter into the night} that is, He is the One who disposes freely over creation, turning the night and the day about and ordaining their measure by His wisdom as He wills. Sometimes He lengthens the night and shortens the day, sometimes the reverse, and sometimes He leaves them equal. And sometimes the season is winter, then spring, then summer, then autumn, and all of that is by His wisdom and His decree, for what He wills of His creation. {And He is Knowing of that within the breasts} that is, He knows secrets even if they are minute, even if they are hidden.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يخبر تعالى عن خلقه السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا فِي سِتَّةِ أَيَّامٍ، ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ بِاسْتِوَائِهِ عَلَى الْعَرْشِ بَعْدَ خَلْقِهِنَّ، وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ الْكَلَامُ عَلَى هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ وَأَشْبَاهِهَا فِي سورة "الأعراف بما أغنى عن إعادته هاهنا.

﴿يَعْلَمُ مَا يَلِجُ فِي الأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: يَعْلَمُ عَدَدَ مَا يَدْخُلُ فِيهَا مِنْ حَبٍّ وَقَطْرٍ ﴿وَمَا يَخْرُجُ مِنْهَا﴾ مِنْ زَرْعٍ ونَبات وَثِمَارٍ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَعِنْدَهُ مَفَاتِحُ الْغَيْبِ لَا يَعْلَمُهَا إِلا هُوَ وَيَعْلَمُ مَا فِي الْبَرِّ وَالْبَحْرِ وَمَا تَسْقُطُ مِنْ وَرَقَةٍ إِلا يَعْلَمُهَا وَلا حَبَّةٍ فِي ظُلُمَاتِ الأرْضِ وَلا رَطْبٍ وَلا يَابِسٍ إِلا فِي كِتَابٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٥٩] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا يَنزلُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْأَمْطَارِ، وَالثُّلُوجِ والبرَد، وَالْأَقْدَارِ وَالْأَحْكَامِ مَعَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ الْكِرَامِ، وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي سُورَةِ "الْبَقَرَةِ" أَنَّهُ مَا يَنْزِلُ مِنْ قَطْرَةٍ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ إِلَّا وَمَعَهَا مَلَكٌ يُقرّرها فِي الْمَكَانِ الَّذِي يَأْمُرُ اللَّهُ بِهِ حَيْثُ يَشَاءُ تَعَالَى.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا يَعْرُجُ فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ وَالْأَعْمَالِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ: "يُرْفَعُ إِلَيْهِ عَمَلُ اللَّيْلِ قَبْلَ النَّهَارِ، وَعَمَلُ النَّهَارِ قَبْلَ اللَّيْلِ" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَهُوَ مَعَكُمْ أَيْنَ مَا كُنْتُمْ وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ بَصِيرٌ﴾ أَيْ: رَقِيبٌ عَلَيْكُمْ، شَهِيدٌ عَلَى أَعْمَالِكُمْ حَيْثُ أَنْتُمْ، وَأَيْنَ كُنْتُمْ، مِنْ بَرٍّ أَوْ بَحْرٍ، فِي لَيْلٍ أَوْ نَهَارٍ، فِي الْبُيُوتِ أَوِ الْقِفَارِ، الْجَمِيعُ فِي عِلْمِهِ عَلَى السَّوَاءِ، وَتَحْتَ بَصَرِهِ وَسَمِعِهِ، فَيَسْمَعُ كَلَامَكُمْ وَيَرَى مَكَانَكُمْ، وَيَعْلَمُ سِرَّكُمْ وَنَجْوَاكُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿أَلا إِنَّهُمْ يَثْنُونَ صُدُورَهُمْ لِيَسْتَخْفُوا مِنْهُ أَلا حِينَ يَسْتَغْشُونَ ثِيَابَهُمْ يَعْلَمُ مَا يُسِرُّونَ وَمَا يُعْلِنُونَ إِنَّهُ عَلِيمٌ بِذَاتِ الصُّدُورِ﴾ [هُودٍ: ٥] . وَقَالَ ﴿سَوَاءٌ مِنْكُمْ مَنْ أَسَرَّ الْقَوْلَ وَمَنْ جَهَرَ بِهِ وَمَنْ هُوَ مُسْتَخْفٍ بِاللَّيْلِ وَسَارِبٌ بِالنَّهَارِ﴾ [الرَّعْدِ: ١٠] ، فَلَا إِلَهَ غَيْرُهُ وَلَا رَبَّ سِوَاهُ. وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ سَلَّمَ قَالَ لِجِبْرِيلَ، لَمَّا سَأَلَهُ عَنِ الْإِحْسَانُ: "أَنْ تَعْبُدَ اللَّهَ كَأَنَّكَ تَرَاهُ، فَإِنْ لَمْ تَكُنْ تَرَاهُ فَإِنَّهُ يَرَاكَ".

وَرَوَى الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْإِسْمَاعِيلِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ نَصْرِ بْنِ خُزَيْمَةَ بْنِ جُنَادَةَ بْنِ مَحْفُوظِ بْنِ عَلْقَمَةَ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، عَنْ نَصْرِ بْنِ عَلْقَمَةَ، عَنْ أَخِيهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ عَائِذٍ قَالَ: قَالَ عُمَرَ: جَاءَ رَجُلٌ إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: زَوِّدْنِي كَلِمَةً أَعِيشُ بِهَا فَقَالَ: "اسْتَحِ اللَّهَ كَمَا تَسْتَحِي رَجُلًا مِنْ صَالِح عَشِيرَتِكَ لَا يُفَارِقُكَ" 

هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ، وَرَوَى أَبُو نُعَيْمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مُعَاوِيَةَ الْغَاضِرِيِّ مَرْفُوعًا: "ثَلَاثٌ مَنْ فَعَلَهُنَّ فَقَدْ طَعِمَ الْإِيمَانَ: مَنْ عَبَدَ اللَّهَ وَحْدَهُ، وَأَعْطَى زَكَاةَ مَالِهِ طَيِّبَةً بِهَا نَفْسُهُ فِي كُلِّ عَامٍ، وَلَمْ يُعْطِ الهَرَمة وَلَا الدَرنة، وَلَا الشَّرط اللَّئِيمَةَ وَلَا الْمَرِيضَةَ وَلَكِنْ مِنْ أَوْسَطِ أَمْوَالِكُمْ. وَزَكَّى نَفْسَه" وَقَالَ رَجُلٌ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا تَزْكِيَةُ الْمَرْءِ نَفْسَهُ؟ فَقَالَ: "يَعْلَمُ أَنَّ اللَّهَ مَعَهُ حَيْثُ كَانَ" 

وَقَالَ نُعَيْم بْنُ حَمّاد، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا عُثْمَانُ بْنُ سَعِيدِ بْنِ كَثِيرِ بْنِ دِينَارِ الْحِمْصِيُّ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ مُهَاجِرٍ، عَنْ عُرْوَةَ بْنُ رُوَيم، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ غَنم، عَنْ عُبَادَةَ بْنِ الصَّامِتِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: " إِنَّ أَفْضَلَ الْإِيمَانِ أَنْ تَعْلَمَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ مَعَكَ حَيْثُمَا كنت". غريب. وَكَانَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ يُنْشِدُ هَذَيْنَ الْبَيْتَيْنِ:

إِذَا مَا خَلَوْتَ الدَّهْرَ يَوْمًا فَلا تَقُلْ ... خَلَوْتُ وَلَكِنْ قُلْ: عَلَيَّ رَقِيبُ ...

وَلا تَحْسَبَنَّ اللهَ يَغْفَلُ سَاعَةً ... وَلا أَنَّ مَا يَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ يَغِيبُ ...

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَهُ مُلْكُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ وَإِلَى اللَّهِ تُرْجَعُ الأمُورُ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ الْمَالِكُ لِلدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِنَّ لَنَا لَلآخِرَةَ وَالأولَى﴾ [اللَّيْلِ: ١٣] ، وَهُوَ الْمَحْمُودُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَهُوَ اللَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا هُوَ لَهُ الْحَمْدُ فِي الأولَى وَالآخِرَةِ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ:٧٠] ، وَقَالَ ﴿الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي لَهُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الأرْضِ وَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ فِي الآخِرَةِ وَهُوَ الْحَكِيمُ الْخَبِيرُ﴾ [سَبَإٍ: ١] . فَجَمِيعُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ مِلْكٌ لَهُ، وَأَهْلُهُمَا عَبِيدٌ أَرِقَّاءُ أَذِلَّاءُ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنْ كُلُّ مَنْ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ إِلا آتِي الرَّحْمَنِ عَبْدًا لَقَدْ أَحْصَاهُمْ وَعَدَّهُمْ عَدًّا وَكُلُّهُمْ آتِيهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فَرْدًا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ: ٩٣-٩٥] . وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِلَى اللَّهِ تُرْجَعُ الأمُورُ﴾ أَيْ: إِلَيْهِ الْمَرْجِعُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَيَحْكُمُ فِي خَلْقِهِ بِمَا يَشَاءُ، وَهُوَ الْعَادِلُ الَّذِي لَا يَجُورُ وَلَا يَظْلِمُ مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ، بَلْ إِنْ يَكُنْ أَحَدُهُمْ عَمِلَ حَسَنَةً وَاحِدَةً يُضَاعِفْهَا إِلَى عَشْرِ أَمْثَالِهَا، ﴿وَيُؤْتِ مِنْ لَدُنْهُ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ٤٠] وَكَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَنَضَعُ الْمَوَازِينَ الْقِسْطَ لِيَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ فَلا تُظْلَمُ نَفْسٌ شَيْئًا وَإِنْ كَانَ مِثْقَالَ حَبَّةٍ مِنْ خَرْدَلٍ أَتَيْنَا بِهَا وَكَفَى بِنَا حَاسِبِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ٤٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يُولِجُ اللَّيْلَ فِي النَّهَارِ وَيُولِجُ النَّهَارَ فِي اللَّيْلِ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ الْمُتَصَرِّفُ فِي الْخَلْقِ، يُقَلِّبُ اللَّيْلَ وَالنَّهَارَ وَيُقَدِّرُهُمَا بِحِكْمَتِهِ كَمَا يَشَاءُ، فَتَارَةً يُطَوِّلُ اللَّيْلَ وَيُقَصِّرُ النَّهَارَ، وَتَارَةً بِالْعَكْسِ، وَتَارَةً يَتْرُكُهُمَا مُعْتَدِلَيْنَ. وَتَارَةً يَكُونُ الْفَصْلُ شِتَاءً ثُمَّ رَبِيعًا ثُمَّ قَيْظًا ثُمَّ خَرِيفًا، وَكُلُّ ذَلِكَ بِحِكْمَتِهِ وَتَقْدِيرِهِ لِمَا يُرِيدُهُ بِخَلْقِهِ، ﴿وَهُوَ عَلِيمٌ بِذَاتِ الصُّدُورِ﴾ أَيْ: يَعْلَمُ السَّرَائِرَ وَإِنْ دَقَّتْ، وَإِنْ خَفِيَتْ.

---

## 57:7-11 — verses 7-11 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted, commanded belief in Him and in His Messenger in the most complete form, with constancy, firmness, and continuance upon that. He urged spending from that which He made you successive trustees over, meaning from what is with you on loan, for it was in the hands of those before you, then it came to you. So He, exalted, guided them to use the wealth over which He had made them trustees in obedience to Him. If they do so, well and good, otherwise He will call them to account for it and punish them for neglecting the obligations attached to it.

Concerning His saying, {of that which He has made you successive trustees over}, there is an indication that it will pass on from you, leaving you behind. Perhaps your heir will obey God with it, and thus be more fortunate with the favor God bestowed upon you than you yourself were, or he may disobey God with it, in which case you will have striven in aiding him toward sin and transgression.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Mutarrif, that is the son of Abd Allah ibn al-Shikhkhir, from his father, who said: I came to the Messenger of God ﷺ while he was saying: "{Rivalry in worldly increase diverts you} [al-Takathur 102:1]. The son of Adam says: my wealth, my wealth! But do you have anything of your wealth except what you ate and thereby consumed, or what you wore and thereby wore out, or what you gave in charity and thereby sent forward?"

Muslim narrated it from the hadith of Shu'bah with the same chain, adding: "and whatever is besides that is going away and he leaves it for other people."

Concerning His saying, {So those among you who believed and spent will have a great reward}, this is an encouragement to belief and to spending in obedience.

Then He said, {And what is with you that you do not believe in God, while the Messenger calls you to believe in your Lord?} That is: what is it that prevents you from belief, when the Messenger is present among you, calling you to it and making clear to you the proofs and evidences for the truth of what he has brought you? We have related, in the hadith, through several chains, at the beginning of the commentary on the "Book of Faith" from Sahih al-Bukhari, that the Messenger of God ﷺ said one day to his companions: "Which of the believers do you find most wondrous in faith?" They said: the angels. He said: "How should they not believe, when they are with their Lord?" They said: then the prophets. He said: "How should they not believe, when revelation descends upon them?" They said: then us? He said: "How should you not believe, when I am present among you? But the most wondrous of believers in faith are a people who will come after you, finding written pages and believing in what is in them."

We have already mentioned a portion of this at the beginning of Surat al-Baqarah, regarding His saying, {Who believe in the unseen} [al-Baqarah 2:3].

Concerning His saying, {and He has taken your covenant}, this is as He said, {And remember the favor of God upon you and His covenant with which He bound you, when you said: we heard and we obeyed} [al-Ma'idah 5:7]. What is meant by this is the pledge of allegiance to the Messenger ﷺ.

Ibn Jarir claimed that what is meant by this is the covenant taken from them in the loins of Adam (peace be upon him), and this is the view of Mujahid as well. God knows best.

Concerning His saying, {It is He who sends down upon His servant clear verses}, that is, clear proofs, dazzling evidences, and decisive demonstrations, {that He may bring you out from darkness into light}, that is, from the darknesses of ignorance, disbelief, and conflicting opinions into the light of guidance, certainty, and faith. {And indeed God is, to you, most Kind and Merciful}, that is, in sending down the books and dispatching the messengers to guide people, remove excuses, and dispel doubts.

Since He had first commanded them to believe and to spend, then urged them to believe and made clear that He had removed the obstacles to it, He also urged them to spend. So He said, {And what is with you that you do not spend in the way of God, while to God belongs the inheritance of the heavens and the earth?} That is: spend and do not fear poverty or want, for the One in whose path you spend is the owner of the heavens and the earth, in whose hand are their keys, and with whom are their treasuries. He is the owner of the Throne and all it encompasses. And He is the one who said, {And whatever you spend of anything, He will replace it, and He is the best of providers} [Saba' 34:39], and He said, {What is with you comes to an end, but what is with God remains} [al-Nahl 16:96]. So whoever relies upon God spends, not fearing want from the Possessor of the Throne, knowing that God will replace it for him.

Concerning His saying, {Not equal among you are those who spent before the conquest and fought}, that is: this person is not equal to one who did not act as he acted. This is because before the conquest of Mecca the situation was severe, and at that time only the most sincere and truthful believed. But after the conquest, Islam appeared with great manifestation, and people entered the religion of God in crowds. For this reason He said, {those are greater in degree than those who spent afterward and fought, though God has promised each a good reward}.

The majority hold that what is meant by "the conquest" here is the conquest of Mecca. It is reported from al-Sha'bi and others that what is meant by "the conquest" here is the truce of al-Hudaybiyyah. This view may be supported by what Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] from Anas, who said: there was an exchange of words between Khalid ibn al-Walid and Abd al-Rahman ibn Awf. Khalid said to Abd al-Rahman: do you claim superiority over us because of days in which you preceded us? It reached us that this was mentioned to the Prophet ﷺ, and he said: "Leave my companions alone for me. By the One in whose hand is my soul, if you were to spend the like of Uhud, or the like of the mountains, in gold, you would not reach the level of their deeds."

It is known that the Islam of Khalid ibn al-Walid, who was addressed by this statement, occurred between the truce of al-Hudaybiyyah and the conquest of Mecca. This dispute between them took place concerning Banu Jadhimah, to whom the Messenger of God ﷺ sent Khalid ibn al-Walid after the conquest. They began saying, "saba'na, saba'na" (we have turned away from our religion), not managing to say properly, "aslamna" (we have submitted). So Khalid ordered that they be killed, including those taken captive among them. Abd al-Rahman ibn Awf and Abd Allah ibn Umar and others opposed him in this, and Khalid and Abd al-Rahman disputed over this matter.

What is established in the Sahih from the Messenger of God ﷺ is that he said: "Do not revile my companions. By the One in whose hand is my soul, if one of you were to spend the like of Uhud in gold, it would not reach the mudd of one of them, nor half of it."

Ibn Jarir and Ibn Abi Hatim narrated, from the hadith of Ibn Wahb: [chain] from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, who said: we set out with the Messenger of God ﷺ in the year of al-Hudaybiyyah, until when we were at Usfan, the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "There will soon come a people whose deeds will make you regard your own deeds as insignificant in comparison." We said: who are they, O Messenger of God, Quraysh? He said: "No, but the people of Yemen. They are more tender of heart and softer of feeling." We said: are they better than us, O Messenger of God? He said: "If one of them had a mountain of gold and spent it, he would not attain the mudd of one of you nor half of it. Indeed, this is the excess that exists between us and other people, {Not equal among you are those who spent before the conquest and fought. Those are greater in degree than those who spent afterward and fought, though God has promised each a good reward, and God is well acquainted with what you do}."

This hadith is gharib (singular) in this wording. What is established in the two Sahihs, through the narration of a group, from Ata' ibn Yasar, from Abu Sa'id, mentions the Khawarij: "You will regard your prayer as insignificant compared to their prayer, and your fasting compared to their fasting. They will pass out of the religion just as an arrow passes through its target," and the rest of the hadith. But Ibn Jarir narrated this hadith by another route, saying:

[chain] from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri: that the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "There will soon come a people whose deeds will make you regard your own deeds as insignificant." We said: who are they, O Messenger of God, Quraysh? He said: "No, but the people of Yemen, for they are more tender of heart and softer of feeling," and he pointed with his hand toward Yemen, saying: "They are the people of Yemen. Indeed faith is Yemeni, and wisdom is Yemeni." We said: O Messenger of God, are they better than us? He said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, if one of them had a mountain of gold and spent it, he would not fulfill the mudd of one of you, nor half of it." Then he brought his fingers together and extended his little finger, and said: "Indeed this is the excess that exists between us and other people, {Not equal among you are those who spent before the conquest and fought. Those are greater in degree than those who spent afterward and fought, though God has promised each a good reward, and God is well acquainted with what you do}."

This context does not mention the Treaty of al-Hudaybiyyah at all. If that report is authentically preserved, as mentioned previously, it is possible that this verse was revealed before the conquest, informing of what would come after it, just as in His statement, exalted is He, in Surat al-Muzzammil, which is Meccan, from among the earliest revelations: {And others who fight in the path of Allah} [al-Muzzammil: 20]. That verse is glad tidings of what would come in the future, and likewise is this one, and Allah knows best.

His statement, {And to each Allah has promised the best reward}, means the ones who spent before the conquest and after it. All of them have a reward for what they did, even though there is a disparity among them in the excellence of the recompense, as He said: {The believers who sit at home, other than those who suffer harm, are not equal to those who strive in the path of Allah with their wealth and their lives. Allah has preferred those who strive with their wealth and their lives over those who sit at home by a degree, and to each Allah has promised the best reward, but Allah has preferred the strivers over those who sit at home with a great reward} [al-Nisa: 95]. Likewise the hadith found in the Sahih: "The strong believer is better and more beloved to Allah than the weak believer, and in each there is good." He only pointed this out so that the side of the other would not be neglected by praising the first without the other, lest someone imagine that this is a disparagement of him. Therefore He followed it with praise and commendation of the other, along with preference of the first over him. This is why He said: {And Allah is well acquainted with what you do}, meaning, because of His full knowledge, He differentiated between the reward of one who spent and fought before the conquest and one who did that afterward. That is only because of His knowledge of the intention and complete sincerity of the first, and his spending in a state of hardship, scarcity, and constraint. In the hadith: "A single dirham surpassed a hundred thousand." There is no doubt among the people of faith that al-Siddiq Abu Bakr, may Allah be pleased with him, has the greatest share of this verse, for he is the master of all who acted upon it among the followers of all the prophets' nations. He spent all of his wealth seeking the countenance of Allah, mighty and majestic is He, and no one had ever done him a favor that he was repaying.

Abu Muhammad al-Husayn ibn Mas'ud al-Baghawi said, when interpreting this verse: [chain] Ibn Umar said: I was with the Prophet ﷺ, and with him was Abu Bakr al-Siddiq, wearing a cloak that he had pinned together over his chest with pins. Then Gabriel (peace be upon him) descended and said: "Why do I see Abu Bakr wearing a cloak pinned together over his chest with pins?" He said: "He spent his wealth on me before the conquest." He said: "Allah says: recite the greeting of peace to him, and say to him: are you pleased with Me in this poverty of yours, or are you displeased?" So the Messenger of Allah said: "O Abu Bakr, Allah conveys the greeting of peace to you, and says to you: are you pleased with Me in this poverty of yours, or are you displeased?" Abu Bakr, may Allah be pleased with him, said: "Should I be displeased with my Lord, mighty and majestic is He? I am indeed pleased with my Lord."

This hadith is weak in its chain of transmission from this route.

Concerning His statement, {Who is it that will lend Allah a goodly loan}, Umar ibn al-Khattab said: it refers to spending in the path of Allah. It has also been said that it refers to spending on one's dependents. The correct view is that it is more general than that: everyone who spends in the path of Allah with a sincere intention and a truthful resolve falls within the general scope of this verse. This is why He said: {Who is it that will lend Allah a goodly loan so that He may multiply it for him}, just as He said in another verse: {manifold multiplications, and Allah withholds and grants abundantly, and to Him you will be returned} [al-Baqarah: 245], meaning: a beautiful recompense and a dazzling provision, which is Paradise, on the Day of Resurrection.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abdullah ibn Mas'ud said: When this verse was revealed, {Who is it that will lend Allah a goodly loan so that He may multiply it for him}, Abu al-Dahdah al-Ansari said: "O Messenger of Allah, does Allah indeed want a loan from us?" He said: "Yes, O Abu al-Dahdah." He said: "Show me your hand, O Messenger of Allah." So he gave him his hand. He said: "I have then lent my Lord my garden," and he had a garden containing six hundred palm trees, in which Umm al-Dahdah and her children lived. Abu al-Dahdah came and called out: "O Umm al-Dahdah!" She said: "Here I am." He said: "Come out, for I have lent it to my Lord, mighty and majestic is He." In another narration, she said to him: "Your transaction has profited, O Abu al-Dahdah," and she moved her belongings and her children out of it. And the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "How many a heavily laden palm branch there is for Abu al-Dahdah in Paradise." In another wording: "Many a dangling palm tree whose roots are pearl and ruby awaits Abu al-Dahdah in Paradise."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَمَرَ تَعَالَى بِالْإِيمَانِ بِهِ وَبِرَسُولِهِ عَلَى الْوَجْهِ الْأَكْمَلِ، وَالدَّوَامِ وَالثَّبَاتِ عَلَى ذَلِكَ وَالِاسْتِمْرَارِ، وَحَثَّ عَلَى الْإِنْفَاقِ مِمَّا جَعَلَكُمْ مُسْتَخْلَفِينَ فِيهِ أَيْ مِمَّا هُوَ مَعَكُمْ عَلَى سَبِيلِ الْعَارِيَةِ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ كَانَ فِي أَيْدِي مَنْ قَبْلَكُمْ ثُمَّ صَارَ إِلَيْكُمْ، فَأَرْشَدَ تَعَالَى إِلَى اسْتِعْمَالِ مَا اسْتَخْلَفَهُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الْمَالِ فِي طَاعَتِهِ، فَإِنْ يَفْعَلُوا وَإِلَّا حَاسَبَهُمْ عَلَيْهِ وَعَاقَبَهُمْ لِتَرْكِهِمُ الْوَاجِبَاتِ فِيهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مِمَّا جَعَلَكُمْ مُسْتَخْلَفِينَ فِيهِ﴾ فِيهِ إِشَارَةٌ إِلَى أَنَّهُ سَيَكُونُ مُخَلَّفًا عَنْكَ، فَلَعَلَّ وَارِثَكَ أَنْ يُطِيعَ اللَّهَ فِيهِ، فَيَكُونَ أَسْعَدَ بِمَا أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ بِهِ عَلَيْكَ مِنْكَ، أَوْ يَعْصِيَ اللَّهَ فِيهِ فَتَكُونَ قَدْ سَعَيْتَ فِي مُعَاوَنَتِهِ عَلَى الْإِثْمِ وَالْعُدْوَانِ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، سَمِعْتُ قَتَادَةَ يُحَدِّثُ، عَنْ مُطَرَّف-يَعْنِي بْنَ عَبْدِ الله بن الشخير-عن أبيه قَالَ: انْتَهَيْتُ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: " ﴿أَلْهَاكُمُ التَّكَاثُرُ﴾ [التَّكَاثُرِ:١] ، يَقُولُ ابْنُ آدَمَ: مَالِي مَالِي! وَهَلْ لَكَ مِنْ مَالِكَ إِلَّا مَا أَكَلْتَ فَأَفْنَيْتَ، أَوْ لَبِسْتَ فَأَبْلَيْتَ، أَوْ تَصَدَّقْتَ فَأَمْضَيْتَ؟ ".

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ مِنْ حَدِيثِ شُعْبَةَ، بِهِ وَزَادَ: "وَمَا سِوَى ذَلِكَ فَذَاهِبٌ وَتَارِكُهُ لِلنَّاسِ"

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مِنْكُمْ وَأَنْفَقُوا لَهُمْ أَجْرٌ كَبِيرٌ﴾ تَرْغِيبٌ فِي الْإِيمَانِ وَالْإِنْفَاقِ فِي الطَّاعَةِ،

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿وَمَا لَكُمْ لَا تُؤْمِنُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَالرَّسُولُ يَدْعُوكُمْ لِتُؤْمِنُوا بِرَبِّكُمْ﴾ ؟ أَيْ: وَأَيُّ شَيْءٍ يَمْنَعُكُمْ مِنَ الْإِيمَانِ وَالرَّسُولُ بَيْنَ أَظْهُرِكُمْ، يَدْعُوكُمْ إِلَى ذَلِكَ وَيُبَيِّنُ لَكُمُ الْحُجَجَ وَالْبَرَاهِينَ عَلَى صِحَّةِ مَا جَاءَكُمْ بِهِ؟ وَقَدْ رَوَيْنَا فِي الْحَدِيثِ مِنْ طُرُق فِي أَوَائِلَ شَرْحِ "كِتَابِ الْإِيمَانِ" مِنْ صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم قَالَ يَوْمًا لِأَصْحَابِهِ: "أيُّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَعْجَبُ إِلَيْكُمْ إِيمَانًا؟ " قَالُوا: الْمَلَائِكَةُ. قَالَ: "وَمَا لَهُمْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ وَهُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ؟ " قَالُوا: فَالْأَنْبِيَاءُ. قَالَ: "وَمَا لَهُمْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ وَالْوَحْيُ يَنْزِلُ عَلَيْهِمْ؟ ". قَالُوا: فَنَحْنُ؟ قَالَ: "وَمَا لَكَمَ لَا تُؤْمِنُونَ وَأَنَا بَيْنَ أَظْهُرِكُمْ؟ وَلَكِنْ أَعْجَبُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ إِيمَانًا قَوْمٌ يجيؤون بَعْدِكُمْ يَجِدُونَ صُحُفًا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِمَا فِيهَا" 

وَقَدْ ذَكَرْنَا طَرَفًا مِنْ هَذَا فِي أَوَّلِ سُورَةِ "الْبَقَرَةِ" عِنْدَ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿الَّذِينَ يُؤْمِنُونَ بِالْغَيْبِ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقَدْ أَخَذَ مِيثَاقَكُمْ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَاذْكُرُوا نِعْمَةَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ وَمِيثَاقَهُ الَّذِي وَاثَقَكُمْ بِهِ إِذْ قُلْتُمْ سَمِعْنَا وَأَطَعْنَا﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ:٧] . وَيَعْنِي بِذَلِكَ: بَيْعَةَ الرَّسُولِ ﷺ.

وَزَعَمَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بِذَلِكَ الْمِيثَاقُ الَّذِي أُخِذَ عَلَيْهِمْ فِي صُلْبِ آدَمَ، وَهُوَ مَذْهَبُ مُجَاهِدٍ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿هُوَ الَّذِي يُنزلُ عَلَى عَبْدِهِ آيَاتٍ بَيِّنَاتٍ﴾ أَيْ: حُجَجًا وَاضِحَاتٍ، وَدَلَائِلَ بَاهِرَاتٍ، وَبَرَاهِينَ قَاطِعَاتٍ، ﴿لِيُخْرِجَكُمْ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ إِلَى النُّورِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ ظُلُمَاتِ الْجَهْلِ وَالْكُفْرِ والآراء الْمُتَضَادَّةِ إِلَى نُورِ الْهُدَى وَالْيَقِينِ وَالْإِيمَانِ، ﴿وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ بِكُمْ لَرَءُوفٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: فِي إِنْزَالِهِ الْكُتُبَ وَإِرْسَالِهِ الرُّسُلَ لِهِدَايَةِ النَّاسِ، وَإِزَاحَةِ الْعِلَلِ وَإِزَالَةِ الشُّبَهِ.

وَلَمَّا أَمَرَهُمْ أَوَّلًا بِالْإِيمَانِ وَالْإِنْفَاقِ، ثُمَّ حَثَّهُمْ عَلَى الْإِيمَانِ، وَبَيَّنَ أَنَّهُ قَدْ أَزَالَ عَنْهُمْ مَوَانِعَهُ، حَثَّهُمْ أَيْضًا عَلَى الْإِنْفَاقِ. فَقَالَ: ﴿وَمَا لَكُمْ أَلا تُنْفِقُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَلِلَّهِ مِيرَاثُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: أَنْفَقُوا وَلَا تخشَوا فَقْرًا وَإِقْلَالًا فَإِنَّ الَّذِي أَنْفَقْتُمْ في سبيله هو مالك السموات وَالْأَرْضِ، وَبِيَدِهِ مَقَالِيدُهُمَا، وَعِنْدَهُ خَزَائِنُهُمَا، وَهُوَ مَالِكُ الْعَرْشِ بِمَا حَوَى، وَهُوَ الْقَائِلُ: ﴿وَمَا أَنْفَقْتُمْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ فَهُوَ يُخْلِفُهُ وَهُوَ خَيْرُ الرَّازِقِينَ﴾ [سَبَإٍ:٣٩] ، وَقَالَ ﴿مَا عِنْدَكُمْ يَنْفَدُ وَمَا عِنْدَ اللَّهِ بَاقٍ﴾ [النَّحْلِ:٩٦] فَمَنْ تَوَكَّلَ عَلَى اللَّهِ أَنْفَقَ، وَلَمْ يَخْشَ مِنْ ذِي الْعَرْشِ إِقْلَالًا وَعَلِمَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ سَيُخْلِفُهُ عَلَيْهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَا يَسْتَوِي مِنْكُمْ مَنْ أَنْفَقَ مِنْ قَبْلِ الْفَتْحِ وَقَاتَلَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَسْتَوِي هَذَا وَمَنْ لَمْ يَفْعَلْ كَفِعْلِهِ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ قَبْلَ فَتْحِ مَكَّةَ كَانَ الْحَالُ شَدِيدًا، فَلَمْ يَكُنْ يُؤْمِنُ حِينَئِذٍ إِلَّا الصِّدِّيقُونَ، وَأَمَّا بَعْدَ الْفَتْحِ فَإِنَّهُ ظَهَرَ الْإِسْلَامُ ظُهُورًا عَظِيمًا، وَدَخَلَ النَّاسُ فِي دِينِ اللَّهِ أَفْوَاجًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ أَعْظَمُ دَرَجَةً مِنَ الَّذِينَ أَنْفَقُوا مِنْ بَعْدُ وَقَاتَلُوا وَكُلا وَعَدَ اللَّهُ الْحُسْنَى﴾

وَالْجُمْهُورُ عَلَى أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بالفتح هاهنا فَتْحُ مَكَّةَ. وَعَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ وَغَيْرِهِ أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بالفتح هاهنا: صُلْحُ الْحُدَيْبِيَةِ، وَقَدْ يُسْتَدَلُّ لِهَذَا الْقَوْلِ بِمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ، حَدَّثَنَا زُهَير، حَدَّثَنَا حُمَيد الطَّوِيلُ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ قَالَ: كَانَ بَيْنَ خَالِدِ بْنِ الْوَلِيدِ وَبَيْنَ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ عَوْفٍ كَلَامٌ، فَقَالَ خَالِدٌ لِعَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ: تَسْتَطِيلُونَ عَلَيْنَا بِأَيَّامٍ سَبَقْتُمُونَا بِهَا؟ فَبَلَغَنَا أَنَّ ذَلِكَ ذُكر لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: " دَعُوا لِي أَصْحَابِي فَوَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَوْ أَنْفَقْتُمْ مِثْلَ أُحُدٍ-أَوْ مِثْلَ الْجِبَالِ-ذَهَبًا، مَا بَلَغْتُمْ أَعْمَالَهُمْ" 

وَمَعْلُومٌ أَنَّ إِسْلَامَ خَالِدِ بْنِ الْوَلِيدِ الْمُوَاجِهِ بِهَذَا الْخِطَابِ كَانَ بَيْنَ صُلْحِ الْحُدَيْبِيَةِ وَفَتْحِ مَكَّةَ، وَكَانَتْ هَذِهِ الْمُشَاجَرَةُ بَيْنَهُمَا فِي بَنِي جَذيمة الَّذِينَ بَعَثَ إِلَيْهِمْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ خَالِدَ بْنَ الْوَلِيدِ بَعْدَ الْفَتْحِ، فَجَعَلُوا يَقُولُونَ: "صَبَأْنَا، صَبَأْنَا"، فَلَمْ يُحْسِنُوا أَنْ يَقُولُوا: "أَسْلَمْنَا"، فَأَمَرَ خَالِدٌ بِقَتْلِهِمْ وَقَتْلِ مَنْ أُسِرِ مِنْهُمْ، فَخَالَفَهُ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ عَوْفٍ، وَعَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عُمَرَ وَغَيْرُهُمَا. فَاخْتَصَمَ خَالِدٌ وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بِسَبَبِ ذَلِكَ 

وَالَّذِي فِي الصَّحِيحِ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: " لَا تَسُبُّوا أَصْحَابِي، فَوَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَوْ أَنْفَقَ أَحَدُكُمْ مِثْلَ أُحُدٍ ذَهَبًا، مَا بَلَغَ مُدّ أَحَدِهِمْ وَلَا نَصيفه" 

وَرَوَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ وَهْبٍ: أَخْبَرَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، عن زيد بن أَسْلَمَ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَارٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: خَرَجْنَا مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَامَ الْحُدَيْبِيَةِ، حَتَّى إِذَا كُنَّا بِعُسْفَانَ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يُوشِكُ أَنْ يَأْتِيَ قَوْمٌ تُحَقِّرُونَ أَعْمَالَكُمْ مَعَ أَعْمَالِهِمْ" فَقُلْنَا: مَنْ هُمْ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ أَقُرَيْشٌ؟ قَالَ: لَا وَلَكِنْ أَهْلُ الْيَمَنِ، هُمْ أَرَقُّ أَفْئِدَةً وَأَلْيَنُ قُلُوبًا". فَقُلْنَا: أَهُمْ خَيْرٌ مِنَّا يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "لَوْ كَانَ لِأَحَدِهِمْ جَبَلٌ مِنْ ذَهَبٍ فَأَنْفَقَهُ، مَا أَدْرَكَ مُدّ أَحَدِكُمْ وَلَا نَصيفه، أَلَا إِنَّ هَذَا فَضْلُ مَا بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَ النَّاسِ، ﴿لَا يَسْتَوِي مِنْكُمْ مَنْ أَنْفَقَ مِنْ قَبْلِ الْفَتْحِ وَقَاتَلَ أُولَئِكَ أَعْظَمُ دَرَجَةً مِنَ الَّذِينَ أَنْفَقُوا مِنْ بَعْدُ وَقَاتَلُوا وَكُلا وَعَدَ اللَّهُ الْحُسْنَى وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ خَبِيرٌ﴾ 

] وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ غَرِيبٌ بِهَذَا السِّيَاقِ، وَالَّذِي فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ جَمَاعَةٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَارٍ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ -ذَكَر الْخَوَارِجَ-: "تَحْقِرُونَ صَلَاتَكُمْ مَعَ صَلَاتِهِمْ، وَصِيَامَكُمْ مَعَ صِيَامِهِمْ، يَمْرُقُونَ مِنَ الدِّينِ كَمَا يَمْرُقُ السَّهْمُ مِنَ الرَّمْيَةِ" الْحَدِيثَ. وَلَكِنْ رَوَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ هَذَا الْحَدِيثَ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ، فَقَالَ:

حَدَّثَنِي بْنُ الْبَرْقِيِّ، حَدَّثَنَا بْنُ أَبِي مَرْيَمَ، أَخْبَرَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي زَيْدُ بْنُ أَسْلَمَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ التَّمَّارِ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "يُوشِكُ أَنْ يَأْتِيَ قَوْمٌ تُحَقِّرُونَ أَعْمَالَكُمْ مَعَ أَعْمَالِهِمْ". قُلْنَا: مَنْ هُمْ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قُرَيْشٌ؟ قَالَ: "لَا وَلَكِنْ أَهْلُ الْيَمَنِ، لِأَنَّهُمْ أَرَقُّ أَفْئِدَةً، وَأَلْيَنُ قُلُوبًا". وَأَشَارَ بِيَدِهِ إِلَى الْيَمَنِ، فَقَالَ: "هُمْ أَهْلُ الْيَمَنِ، أَلَا إِنَّ الْإِيمَانَ يَمَانٍ، وَالْحِكْمَةَ يَمَانِيَةٌ". فَقُلْنَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، هُمْ خَيْرٌ مِنَّا؟ قَالَ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَوْ كَانَ لِأَحَدِهِمْ جَبَلٌ مِنْ ذَهَبٍ يُنْفِقُهُ مَا أَدَّى مُدّ أَحَدِكُمْ وَلَا نَصِيفَهُ". ثُمَّ جَمَعَ أَصَابِعَهُ وَمَدَّ خِنْصَرَهُ، وَقَالَ: "أَلَا إِنَّ هَذَا فضلُ مَا بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَ النَّاسِ، ﴿لَا يَسْتَوِي مِنْكُمْ مَنْ أَنْفَقَ مِنْ قَبْلِ الْفَتْحِ وَقَاتَلَ أُولَئِكَ أَعْظَمُ دَرَجَةً مِنَ الَّذِينَ أَنْفَقُوا مِنْ بَعْدُ وَقَاتَلُوا وَكُلا وَعَدَ اللَّهُ الْحُسْنَى وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ خَبِيرٌ﴾ ] " 

فَهَذَا السِّيَاقُ لَيْسَ فِيهِ ذِكْرُ الْحُدَيْبِيَةِ فَإِنْ كَانَ ذَلِكَ مَحْفُوظًا كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ، فَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنَّهُ أُنْزِلَ قَبْلَ الْفَتْحِ إِخْبَارًا عَمَّا بَعْدَهُ، كَمَا فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى فِي سُورَةِ "الْمُزَّمِّلِ"-وَهِيَ مَكِّيَّةٌ، مِنْ أَوَائِلِ مَا نَزَلَ-: ﴿وَآخَرُونَ يُقَاتِلُونَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْمُزَّمِّلِ: ٢٠] فَهِيَ بِشَارَةٌ بِمَا يُسْتَقْبَلُ، وَهَكَذَا هَذِهِ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكُلا وَعَدَ اللَّهُ الْحُسْنَى﴾ يَعْنِي الْمُنْفِقِينَ قَبْلَ الْفَتْحِ وَبَعْدَهُ، كُلُّهُمْ لَهُمْ ثَوَابٌ عَلَى مَا عَمِلُوا، وَإِنْ كَانَ بَيْنَهُمْ تَفَاوُتٌ فِي تُفَاضُلِ الْجَزَاءِ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿لَا يَسْتَوِي الْقَاعِدُونَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ غَيْرُ أُولِي الضَّرَرِ وَالْمُجَاهِدُونَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ بِأَمْوَالِهِمْ وَأَنْفُسِهِمْ فَضَّلَ اللَّهُ الْمُجَاهِدِينَ بِأَمْوَالِهِمْ وَأَنْفُسِهِمْ عَلَى الْقَاعِدِينَ دَرَجَةً وَكُلا وَعَدَ اللَّهُ الْحُسْنَى وَفَضَّلَ اللَّهُ الْمُجَاهِدِينَ عَلَى الْقَاعِدِينَ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ:٩٥] . وَهَكَذَا الْحَدِيثُ الَّذِي فِي الصَّحِيحِ: "الْمُؤْمِنُ الْقَوِيُّ خَيْرٌ وَأَحَبُّ إِلَى اللَّهِ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِ الضَّعِيفِ، وَفِي كُلٍّ خَيْرٌ" وَإِنَّمَا نَبَّه بِهَذَا لِئَلَّا يُهدرَ جَانِبُ الْآخَرِ بِمَدْحِ الْأَوَّلِ دُونَ الْآخَرِ، فَيَتَوَهَّمُ مُتَوَهِّمٌ ذَمَّهُ؛ فَلِهَذَا عَطَفَ بِمَدْحِ الْآخَرِ وَالثَّنَاءِ عَلَيْهِ، مَعَ تَفْضِيلِ الْأَوَّلِ عَلَيْهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ خَبِيرٌ﴾ أَيْ: فَلِخِبْرَتِهِ فَاوَتَ بَيْنَ ثَوَابِ مَنْ أَنْفَقَ مِنْ قَبْلِ الْفَتْحِ وَقَاتَلَ، وَمَنْ فَعَلَ ذَلِكَ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ، وَمَا ذَلِكَ إِلَّا لِعِلْمِهِ بِقَصْدِ الْأَوَّلِ وَإِخْلَاصِهِ التَّامِّ، وَإِنْفَاقِهِ فِي حَالِ الْجُهْدِ وَالْقِلَّةِ وَالضِّيقِ. وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ: "سَبَقَ دِرْهَمٌ مِائَةَ أَلْفٍ" وَلَا شَكَّ عِنْدَ أَهْلِ الْإِيمَانِ أَنَّ الصِّدِّيقَ أَبَا بَكْرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، لَهُ الْحَظُّ الْأَوْفَرُ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ، فَإِنَّهُ سَيِّدُ مَنْ عَمِلَ بِهَا مِنْ سَائِرِ أُمَمِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، فَإِنَّهُ أَنْفَقَ مَالَهُ كُلَّهُ ابْتِغَاءَ وَجْهِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لِأَحَدٍ عِنْدَهُ نِعْمَةٌ يَجْزِيهِ بِهَا.

وَقَدْ قَالَ أَبُو مُحَمَّدٍ الْحُسَيْنُ بْنُ مَسْعُودٍ الْبَغَوِيُّ عِنْدَ تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ أَخْبَرَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الشُّرَيْحِيُّ أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الثَّعْلَبِيُّ، أَخْبَرَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ حَامِدِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ أَيُّوبَ، أَخْبَرَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ يُونُسَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْعَلَاءُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو الشَّيْبَانِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ الْفَزَارِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ آدَمَ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: كُنْتُ عِنْدَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ وَعِنْدَهُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الصِّدِّيقُ، وَعَلَيْهِ عَبَاءَةٌ قَدْ خَلَّها فِي صَدْرِهِ بِخِلَالٍ، فَنَزَلَ جِبْرِيلُ فَقَالَ: مَالِي أَرَى أَبَا بَكْرٍ عَلَيْهِ عَبَاءَةٌ قَدْ خَلَّها فِي صَدْرِهِ بِخلال؟ فَقَالَ: "أَنْفَقَ مَالَهُ عليَّ قَبْلَ الْفَتْحِ" قَالَ: فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقُولُ: اقْرَأْ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامَ، وَقُلْ لَهُ: أَرَاضٍ أنت عني في فقرك هذا أم ساخط؟ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ: "يَا أَبَا بَكْرٍ، إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقْرَأُ عَلَيْكَ السَّلَامَ، وَيَقُولُ لَكَ: أَرَاضٍ أنت عَني في فقرك هذا أم ساخط؟ " فَقَالَ: أَبُو بَكْرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: أَسْخَطُ عَلَى رَبِّي عَزَّ وَجَلَّ؟ إِنِّي عَنْ رَبِّي رَاضٍ 

هَذَا الْحَدِيثُ ضَعِيفُ الْإِسْنَادِ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يُقْرِضُ اللَّهَ قَرْضًا حَسَنًا﴾ قَالَ عُمَرُ بْنُ الْخَطَّابِ: هُوَ الْإِنْفَاقُ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، وَقِيلَ: هُوَ النَّفَقَةُ عَلَى الْعِيَالِ وَالصَّحِيحُ أَنَّهُ أَعَمُّ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، فَكُلُّ مَنْ أَنْفَقَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ بِنِيَّةٍ خَالِصَةٍ وَعَزِيمَةٍ صَادِقَةٍ، دَخَلَ فِي عُمُومِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يُقْرِضُ اللَّهَ قَرْضًا حَسَنًا فَيُضَاعِفَهُ لَهُ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿أَضْعَافًا كَثِيرَةً وَاللَّهُ يَقْبِضُ وَيَبْصُطُ وَإِلَيْهِ تُرْجَعُونَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٤٥] أَيْ: جَزَاءٌ جَمِيلٌ وَرِزْقٌ بَاهِرٌ-وَهُوَ الْجَنَّةُ-يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ.

قَالَ بْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ عَرَفَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا خَلَفُ بْنُ خَلِيفَةَ، عَنْ حُمَيْدٍ الْأَعْرَجِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يُقْرِضُ اللَّهَ قَرْضًا حَسَنًا فَيُضَاعِفَهُ لَهُ﴾ قَالَ أَبُو الدَّحْدَاحِ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَيُرِيدُ مِنَّا الْقَرْضَ؟ " قَالَ: "نَعَمْ، يَا أَبَا الدَّحْدَاحِ". قَالَ أَرِنِي يَدَكَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ قَالَ: فَنَاوَلَهُ يَدَهُ قَالَ: فَإِنِّي قَدْ أَقْرَضْتُ رَبِّي حَائِطِي-وَلَهُ حَائِطٌ فِيهِ سِتُّمِائَةِ نَخْلَةٍ، وَأُمُّ الدَّحْدَاحِ فِيهِ وَعِيَالُهَا-قال: فجاء أبو الدحداح فنادها: يَا أَمَّ الدَّحْدَاحِ. قَالَتْ: لَبَّيْكَ. فَقَالَ: اخْرُجِي، فَقَدْ أَقْرَضْتُهُ رَبِّي، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ-وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: أَنَّهَا قَالَتْ لَهُ: رَبح بَيْعُكَ يَا أَبَا الدَّحْدَاحِ. وَنَقَلَتْ مِنْهُ مَتَاعَهَا وَصِبْيَانَهَا، وَإِنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "كَمْ مِنْ عَذْق رَدَاح فِي الْجَنَّةِ لِأَبِي الدَّحْدَاحِ". وَفِي لَفْظٍ: "رُبَّ نَخْلَةٍ مُدَلَّاةٍ عُرُوقُهَا دُرٌّ وياقوت لأبي الدحداح في الجنة".

---

## 57:12-15 — verses 12-15 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about the believers who give charity, that on the Day of Resurrection their light will run before them across the plains of the Resurrection, according to their deeds, as Abdullah ibn Mas'ud said concerning His statement: {their light will run before them}, he said: according to the measure of their deeds they will pass over the bridge (al-sirat). Among them is one whose light is like a mountain, among them is one whose light is like a palm tree, among them is one whose light is like a standing man, and the least of them in light is one whose light is in his thumb, flaring up once and going out once. This was related by Ibn Abi Hatim and Ibn Jarir.

Qatadah said: it was mentioned to us that the Prophet of Allah ﷺ used to say: "Among the believers is one whose light shines from Medina to Aden Abyan and Sana'a and beyond that, until there are among the believers those whose light shines no further than the place of their two feet."

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from Husayn, from Mujahid, from Junadah ibn Umayyah, who said: you are recorded with Allah by your names, your marks, your adornments, your secret conversations and your gatherings. When the Day of Resurrection comes it will be said: "O so-and-so, this is your light. O so-and-so, you have no light." Then he recited: {their light will run before them}.

Al-Dahhak said: there is no one who will not be given a light on the Day of Resurrection. When they reach the bridge, the light of the hypocrites will be extinguished. When the believers see this, they will fear that their own light will be extinguished just as the hypocrites' light was extinguished, so they will say: "Our Lord, complete for us our light."

Al-Hasan said, concerning His statement {their light will run before them}: meaning, over the bridge.

Ibn Abi Hatim, may Allah have mercy on him, said: [chain] Abu Ubaydillah, nephew of Ibn Wahb, told us, my uncle informed us, from Yazid ibn Abi Habib, from Sa'id ibn Mas'ud, that he heard Abd al-Rahman ibn Jubayr relate that he heard Abu al-Darda and Abu Dharr report from the Prophet ﷺ that he said: "I am the first for whom permission will be given on the Day of Resurrection to prostrate, and the first for whom permission will be given to raise his head. Then I will look before me, behind me, to my right and to my left, and I will recognize my nation from among the other nations." A man said to him: "O Prophet of Allah, how will you recognize your nation from among the nations, from Noah's time to your nation?" He said: "I will recognize them by the marks left from ablution on their limbs (tahajjul), and no other nation will have that. I will recognize them because their records will be given to them in their right hands, I will recognize them by the marks on their faces, and I will recognize them by their light running before them and before their offspring."

His saying {and in their right hands}: Al-Dahhak said, meaning, and in their right hands will be their records, as He said: {then whoever is given his record in his right hand} [al-Isra 17:71].

His saying {Your good tidings today are gardens beneath which rivers flow}: meaning, it will be said to them: your good tidings today are gardens, that is, you are given the glad tidings of gardens beneath which rivers flow. {Abiding therein eternally}, meaning, remaining in them forever. {That is the great triumph.}

His saying {On the Day when the hypocrite men and hypocrite women will say to those who believed, "Wait for us that we may borrow some of your light"}: this is information from Him, Exalted is He, about what will occur on the Day of Resurrection in the plains, of terrifying calamities, immense tremors, and dreadful matters. None will be saved on that day except one who believed in Allah and His Messenger, acted according to what Allah commanded, and abstained from what He forbade.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] my father told us, Abdah ibn Sulayman told us, Ibn al-Mubarak told us, Safwan ibn Amr told us, Sulaym ibn Amir told me, saying: we went out for a funeral at the gate of Damascus, and with us was Abu Umamah al-Bahili. When he had prayed over the deceased and they began to bury him, Abu Umamah said: "O people, you have risen this morning and passed this evening in a dwelling in which you divide good deeds and bad deeds, and you are soon to depart from it to another dwelling," and he pointed to the grave, "the house of solitude, the house of darkness, the house of worms, the house of narrowness, except for whomever Allah widens it. Then you move from it to the stations of the Day of Resurrection. In some of those stations a matter from Allah will overwhelm the people, so that faces will turn white and faces will turn black. Then you move from there to another dwelling, where intense darkness will overwhelm the people. Then the light will be distributed: the believer will be given a light, while the disbeliever and the hypocrite will be left with nothing given to them. This is the parable that Allah gave in His Book, where He said: {or as darknesses within a sea deep and dark}, up to His saying {he will have no light at all} [al-Nur 24:40]. So the disbeliever and the hypocrite will not be able to see by the light of the believer, just as the blind man cannot see by the light of the sighted man. The hypocrites will say to those who believed: {wait for us that we may borrow some of your light. It will be said: go back and search for light}. This is the deception of Allah with which He deceived the hypocrites, as He said: {they seek to deceive Allah, but He is deceiving them} [al-Nisa 4:142]. So they return to the place where the light was distributed, and find nothing, then they turn back toward the believers, but a wall will already have been placed between them, with a gate, {its inner side containing mercy, and its outer side, facing it, punishment}" the rest of the verse. Sulaym ibn Amir says: the hypocrite remains deceived until the light is distributed and Allah distinguishes between the believer and the hypocrite.

Then Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] my father told us, Yahya ibn Uthman told us, Ibn Hayawah told us, Artah ibn al-Mundhir told us, Yusuf ibn al-Hajjaj told us, from Abu Umamah, who said: darkness will be sent forth on the Day of Resurrection, and neither believer nor disbeliever will be able to see his own palm, until Allah sends light to the believers according to the measure of their deeds. The hypocrites will follow them, saying: {wait for us that we may borrow some of your light}.

Al-Awfi, al-Dahhak and others, from Ibn Abbas, said: while the people are in darkness, Allah will send forth a light. When the believers see the light, they will head toward it, for the light will be a guide from Allah to Paradise. When the hypocrites see the believers set off, they will follow them, but Allah will darken it for the hypocrites, and they will then say: {wait for us that we may borrow some of your light, for we were with you in the world}. The believers will say: {go back} to where you came from in the darkness, and search for light there.

Abu al-Qasim al-Tabarani said: [chain] al-Hasan ibn Allawiyah al-Qattan told us, Isma'il ibn Isa al-Attar told us, Ishaq ibn Bishr Abu Hudhayfah told us, Ibn Jurayj told us, from Ibn Abi Mulaykah, from Ibn Abbas, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah calls the people on the Day of Resurrection by their names, as a veil of His over His servants. But at the bridge, Allah gives every believer a light and every hypocrite a light. When they are all set upon the bridge, Allah strips away the light of the hypocrite men and hypocrite women. The hypocrites will say: {wait for us that we may borrow some of your light}, and the believers will say: {our Lord, complete for us our light} [al-Tahrim 66:8]. At that point no one will remember anyone else." 

His saying {so a wall will be placed between them, with a gate, its inner side containing mercy, and its outer side, facing it, punishment}: al-Hasan and Qatadah said this is a wall between Paradise and the Fire.

Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: this is what Allah, Exalted is He, referred to when He said: {and between them is a veil} [al-A'raf 7:46]. And this has likewise been related from Mujahid, may Allah have mercy on him, and others, and this is the correct view.

{Its inner side containing mercy}, meaning, Paradise and what is in it. {And its outer side, facing it, punishment}, meaning, the Fire. This was said by Qatadah, Ibn Zayd, and others.

Ibn Jarir said: it has been said that this wall is the wall of the Sacred House (Bayt al-Maqdis) beside the valley of Hell. Then he said: [chain] Ibn al-Barqi told us, Amr ibn Abi Salamah told us, from Sa'id ibn Atiyyah ibn Qays, from Abu al-Awwam, the muezzin of the Sacred House, who said: I heard Abdullah ibn Amr say: the wall that Allah mentioned in the Qur'an, {so a wall will be placed between them, with a gate, its inner side containing mercy, and its outer side, facing it, punishment}, is the eastern wall, its inner side being the mosque and what adjoins it, and its outer side being the valley of Hell.

Then something similar was related from Ubadah ibn al-Samit, Ka'b al-Ahbar, and Ali ibn al-Husayn Zayn al-Abidin. This is to be understood from them as intending merely to draw the meaning near through an illustration and example, not that this specific wall, the mosque itself and what lies beyond it of the valley known as the valley of Hell, is truly what is meant by the Qur'an. For Paradise is in the heavens, in the highest of the elevated ranks (Illiyyin), and the Fire is in the depths, in the lowest of the low.

As for the statement of Ka'b al-Ahbar that the gate mentioned in the Qur'an is the Gate of Mercy, which is one of the gates of the mosque, this is one of his Isra'iliyyat (Israelite-derived reports) and idle tales. Rather, what is meant by that is a wall that will be set up on the Day of Resurrection to separate between the believers and the hypocrites. When the believers reach it, they will enter through its gate, and when they have completely entered, the gate will be closed, and the hypocrites will remain behind it in confusion, darkness, and torment, just as they were in the abode of this world in disbelief, ignorance, doubt, and confusion. {They will call out to them: were we not with you?} That is, the hypocrites will call out to the believers: were we not with you in the worldly abode? Did we not attend the Friday prayers with you, pray the congregational prayers with you, stand with you at Arafat, be present with you in the military expeditions, and perform along with you all the rest of the obligatory duties? {They will say: yes indeed}, that is, the believers will answer the hypocrites, saying: yes indeed, you were with us, {but you tempted yourselves, and you waited, and you doubted, and false hopes deluded you}. Some of the Salaf said: that is, you tempted yourselves with pleasures, sins, and desires. {And you waited}, that is, you kept delaying repentance from one time to another.

Qatadah said: {And you waited} concerning the truth and its people, {and you doubted}, that is, concerning the resurrection after death, {and false hopes deluded you}, that is, you used to say, we will be forgiven. And it has also been said: the world deluded you, {until the command of God came}, that is, you remained in this state until death came, {and the deceiver deceived you concerning God}, that is, Satan.

Qatadah said: they were under a deception from Satan. By God, they never ceased to be under it until God cast them into the Fire.

The meaning of these words from the believers to the hypocrites is: you were with us [that is] in bodies without intention and without hearts present with them. Rather, you were in confusion and doubt, showing off to people and remembering God only a little.

Mujahid said: the hypocrites were with the believers in life, intermarrying with them, deceiving them, and associating with them, but in reality they were dead among them. All will be given light together on the Day of Resurrection, but the light of the hypocrites will be extinguished when they reach the wall, and a separation will then be made between them.

This statement from the believers does not contradict what God has related about them elsewhere, where He, the truest of speakers, says: {Every soul is held in pledge for what it has earned, except the companions of the right, in gardens, they will ask one another about the criminals: what led you into Saqar? They will say: we were not among those who prayed, and we did not feed the poor, and we used to indulge in vain talk with those who indulged, and we used to deny the Day of Judgment, until certainty came to us} [al-Muddaththir: 38-47]. This statement issued from them only by way of rebuke and reproach against themselves. Then He, exalted, said: {So the intercession of intercessors will not benefit them} [al-Muddaththir: 48], just as He says here: {So today no ransom will be taken from you, nor from those who disbelieved}, that is, if one of you were to bring today the fill of the earth in gold, and its like along with it, in order to ransom himself from the punishment of God, it would not be accepted from him.

As for His saying: {Your abode is the Fire}, that is, it is your destination and to it is your return.

As for His saying: {It is your protector}, that is, it is more deserving of you than any other dwelling, because of your disbelief and your doubt, and evil is that destination.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبَرًا عَنِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ الْمُتَصَدِّقِينَ: أَنَّهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يسعَى نُورُهُمْ بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ فِي عَرصات الْقِيَامَةِ، بِحَسَبِ أَعْمَالِهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مَسْعُودٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَسْعَى نُورُهُمْ بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ﴾ قَالَ: عَلَى قَدْرِ أَعْمَالِهِمْ يَمُرُّونَ عَلَى الصِّرَاطِ، مِنْهُمْ مَن نُورُهُ مِثْلُ الْجَبَلِ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَن نُورُهُ مِثْلُ النَّخْلَةِ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَن نُورُهُ مِثْلُ الرَّجُلِ الْقَائِمِ، وَأَدْنَاهُمْ نُورًا مَن نُورُهُ فِي إِبْهَامِهِ يتَّقد مَرَّةً وَيُطْفَأُ مَرَّةً ورواه بن أبي حاتم وبن جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ يَقُولُ: "مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ مَنْ يُضِيءُ نُوره مِنَ الْمَدِينَةِ إِلَى عَدن أَبْيَنَ وَصَنْعَاءَ فَدُونَ ذَلِكَ، حَتَّى إِنَّ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ مَنْ يُضِيءُ نُورُهُ مَوْضِعَ قَدَمَيْهِ" 

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ حُصَين، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ عَنْ جُنَادة بْنِ أُمَيَّةَ قَالَ: إِنَّكُمْ مَكُتُوبُونَ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ بِأَسْمَائِكُمْ، وَسِيمَاكُمْ وحُلاكم، وَنَجْوَاكُمْ وَمَجَالِسِكُمْ، فَإِذَا كَانَ يَوْمُ الْقِيَامَةِ قِيلَ: يَا فُلَانُ، هَذَا نُورُكُ. يَا فُلَانُ، لَا نُورَ لَكَ. وَقَرَأَ: ﴿يَسْعَى نُورُهُمْ بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ﴾

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: لَيْسَ لِأَحَدٍ إِلَّا يُعْطَى نُورًا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَإِذَا انْتَهَوْا إِلَى الصِّرَاطِ طُفِئَ نُورُ الْمُنَافِقِينَ، فَلَمَّا رَأَى ذَلِكَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ أَشْفَقُوا أَنْ يُطْفَأَ نُورُهُمْ كَمَا طُفئ نُورُ الْمُنَافِقِينَ، فَقَالُوا: رَبَّنَا، أَتْمِمْ لَنَا نُورَنَا.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ [فِي قَوْلِهِ] ﴿يَسْعَى نُورُهُمْ بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ﴾ يَعْنِي: عَلَى الصراط.

وَقَدْ قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ ابْنُ أَخِي ابْنِ وَهْبٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا عَمِّي عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ أَبِي حَبِيبٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ عَبْدَ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنَ جُبَيْر يُحَدِّثُ: أَنَّهُ سَمِع أَبَا الدَّرْدَاءِ وَأَبَا ذَرٍّ يُخْبِرَانِ عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "أَنَا أَوَّلُ مَنْ يُؤْذَنُ لَهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ بِالسُّجُودِ، وَأَوَّلُ مَنْ يُؤْذَنُ لَهُ بِرَفْعِ رَأْسِهِ، فَأَنْظُرُ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدِي وَمِنْ خَلْفِي، وَعَنْ يَمِينِي وَعَنْ شِمَالِي، فَأَعْرِفُ أُمَّتِي مِنْ بَيْنِ الْأُمَمِ". فَقَالَ لَهُ رَجُلٌ: يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ، كَيْفَ تَعْرِفُ أُمَّتَكَ مِنْ بَيْنِ الْأُمَمِ، مَا بَيْنَ نُوحٍ إِلَى أُمَّتِكَ؟ قَالَ: "أَعْرِفُهُمْ، مُحَجَّلون مِنْ أَثَرِ الْوُضُوءِ، وَلَا يَكُونُ لِأَحَدٍ مِنَ الْأُمَمِ غَيْرِهِمْ، وَأَعْرِفُهُمْ يُؤْتَون كُتُبَهُمْ بِأَيْمَانِهِمْ، وَأَعْرِفُهُمْ بِسِيمَاهُمْ فِي وُجُوهِهِمْ، وَأَعْرِفُهُمْ بِنُورِهِمْ يَسْعَى بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَذُرِّيَّتِهِمْ 

* *
