وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿وَبِأَيْمَانِهِمْ﴾ قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: أَيْ وَبِأَيْمَانِهِمْ كُتُبُهُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿فَمَنْ أُوتِيَ كِتَابَهُ بِيَمِينِهِ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٧١] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بُشْرَاكُمُ الْيَوْمَ جَنَّاتٌ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الأنْهَارُ﴾ أَيْ: يُقَالُ لَهُمْ: بُشْرَاكُمُ الْيَوْمَ جَنَّاتٌ، أَيْ: لَكُمُ الْبِشَارَةُ بِجَنَّاتٍ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ، ﴿خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: مَاكِثِينَ فِيهَا أَبَدًا ﴿ذَلِكَ هُوَ الْفَوْزُ الْعَظِيمُ﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَوْمَ يَقُولُ الْمُنَافِقُونَ وَالْمُنَافِقَاتُ لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا انْظُرُونَا نَقْتَبِسْ مِنْ نُورِكُمْ﴾ وَهَذَا إِخْبَارٌ مِنْهُ تَعَالَى عَمَّا يَقَعُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فِي الْعَرَصَاتِ مِنَ الْأَهْوَالِ الْمُزْعِجَةِ، وَالزَّلَازِلِ الْعَظِيمَةِ، وَالْأُمُورِ الْفَظِيعَةِ وَإِنَّهُ لَا يَنْجُو يَوْمَئِذٍ إِلَّا مَنْ آمَنَ بِاللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ، وَعَمِلَ بِمَا أَمَرَ اللَّهُ، بِهِ وَتَرَكَ مَا عَنْهُ زَجَرَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدَةُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، حَدَّثَنَا صَفْوَانَ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، حَدَّثَنِي سُلَيْمُ بْنُ عَامِرٍ قَالَ: خَرَجْنَا عَلَى جِنَازَةٍ فِي بَابِ دِمَشْقَ، وَمَعَنَا أَبُو أُمَامَةَ الْبَاهِلِيُّ، فَلَمَّا صَلَّى عَلَى الْجِنَازَةِ وَأَخَذُوا فِي دَفْنِهَا، قَالَ أَبُو أُمَامَةَ: أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، إِنَّكُمْ قَدْ أَصْبَحْتُمْ وَأَمْسَيْتُمْ فِي مَنْزِلٍ تَقْتَسِمُونَ فِيهِ الْحَسَنَاتِ وَالسَّيِّئَاتِ، وَتُوشِكُونَ أَنْ تَظْعَنُوا مِنْهُ إِلَى مَنْزِلٍ آخَرَ، وَهُوَ هَذَا-يُشِيرُ إِلَى الْقَبْرِ-بَيْتُ الْوَحْدَةِ، وَبَيْتُ الظُّلْمَةِ، وَبَيْتُ الدُّودِ، وَبَيْتُ الضِّيقِ، إِلَّا مَا وَسَّعَ اللَّهُ، تَنْتَقِلُونَ مِنْهُ إِلَى مُوَاطِنِ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَإِنَّكُمْ فِي بَعْضِ تِلْكَ الْمَوَاطِنِ [حَتَّى] يَغْشَى النَّاسَ أَمْرٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ، فَتَبْيَضَّ وُجُوهٌ وَتَسْوَدَّ وُجُوهٌ، ثُمَّ تَنْتَقِلُونَ مِنْهُ إِلَى مَنْزِلٍ آخَرَ فَتَغْشَى النَّاسَ ظُلْمَةٌ شَدِيدَةٌ، ثُمَّ يُقَسَّمُ النُّورُ فَيُعْطَى الْمُؤْمِنُ نُورًا وَيُتْرَكُ الْكَافِرُ وَالْمُنَافِقُ فَلَا يُعْطَيَانِ شَيْئًا، وَهُوَ الْمَثَلُ الَّذِي ضَرَبَهُ اللَّهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ، قَالَ ﴿أَوْ كَظُلُمَاتٍ فِي بَحْرٍ لُجِّيٍّ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَمَا لَهُ مِنْ نُورٍ﴾ [النُّورِ: ٤٠] ، فَلَا يَسْتَضِيءُ الْكَافِرُ وَالْمُنَافِقُ بِنُورِ الْمُؤْمِنِ كَمَا لَا يَسْتَضِيءُ الْأَعْمَى بِنُورِ الْبَصِيرِ، وَيَقُولُ الْمُنَافِقُونَ لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا: ﴿انْظُرُونَا نَقْتَبِسْ مِنْ نُورِكُمْ قِيلَ ارْجِعُوا وَرَاءَكُمْ فَالْتَمِسُوا نُورًا﴾ وَهِيَ خدعة الله التي خدع بِهَا الْمُنَافِقِينَ حَيْثُ قَالَ: ﴿يُخَادِعُونَ اللَّهَ وَهُوَ خَادِعُهُمْ﴾ [النِّسَاءِ:١٤٢] . فَيَرْجِعُونَ إِلَى الْمَكَانِ الَّذِي قُسِّمَ فِيهِ النُّورُ، فَلَا يَجِدُونَ شَيْئًا فَيَنْصَرِفُونَ إِلَيْهِمْ وَقَدْ ضُرِبَ بَيْنَهُمْ بِسُورٍ لَهُ بَابٌ، ﴿بَاطِنُهُ فِيهِ الرَّحْمَةُ وَظَاهِرُهُ مِنْ قِبَلِهِ الْعَذَابُ﴾ الْآيَةَ. يَقُولُ سُلَيْمُ بْنُ عَامِرٍ: فَمَا يَزَالُ الْمُنَافِقُ مُغْتَرًّا حَتَّى يُقَسَّمَ النُّورُ، وَيُمَيِّزَ اللَّهُ بَيْنَ والمؤمن المنافق.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ عُثْمَانَ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حَيْوَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَرْطَأَةُ بْنُ الْمُنْذِرِ، حَدَّثَنَا يُوسُفُ بْنُ الْحَجَّاجِ، عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ قَالَ: تُبْعَثُ ظُلْمَةٌ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَمَا مِنْ مُؤْمِنٍ وَلَا كَافِرٍ يَرَى كَفَّهُ، حَتَّى يَبْعَثَ اللَّهُ بِالنُّورِ إِلَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِقَدْرِ أَعْمَالِهِمْ، فَيَتْبَعُهُمُ الْمُنَافِقُونَ فَيَقُولُونَ: ﴿انْظُرُونَا نَقْتَبِسْ مِنْ نُورِكُمْ﴾ .

وَقَالَ العَوْفي، وَالْضَّحَّاكُ، وَغَيْرُهُمَا، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: بَيْنَمَا النَّاسُ فِي ظُلْمَةٍ إِذْ بَعَثَ اللَّهُ نُورًا فَلَمَّا رَأْي الْمُؤْمِنُونَ النُّورَ تَوَجَّهُوا نَحْوَهُ، وَكَانَ النُّورُ دَلِيلًا مِنَ اللَّهِ إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ، فَلَمَّا رَأَى الْمُنَافِقُونَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ قَدِ انْطَلَقُوا اتَّبَعُوهُمْ، فَأَظْلَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَى الْمُنَافِقِينَ، فَقَالُوا حِينَئِذٍ: ﴿انْظُرُونَا نَقْتَبِسْ مِنْ نُورِكُمْ﴾ فَإِنَّا كُنَّا مَعَكُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا. قَالَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ﴿ارْجِعُوا﴾ مِنْ حَيْثُ جِئْتُمْ مِنَ الظُّلْمَةِ، فَالْتَمِسُوا هُنَالِكَ النُّورَ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ عَلَّوَيْهِ الْقَطَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ عِيسَى الْعَطَّارُ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ بِشْرٍ أَبُو حُذَيْفَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي مُلَيْكة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَدْعُو النَّاسَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ بِأَسْمَائِهِمْ سِتْرًا مِنْهُ عَلَى عِبَادِهِ، وَأَمَّا عِنْدَ الصِّرَاطِ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يُعْطِي كُلَّ مُؤْمِنٍ نُورًا، وَكُلَّ مُنَافِقٍ نُورًا، فَإِذَا اسْتَوَوْا عَلَى الصِّرَاطِ سَلَبَ اللَّهُ نُورَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ وَالْمُنَافِقَاتِ فَقَالَ الْمُنَافِقُونَ: ﴿انْظُرُونَا نَقْتَبِسْ مِنْ نُورِكُمْ﴾ وَقَالَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ﴿رَبَّنَا أَتْمِمْ لَنَا نُورَنَا﴾ [التَّحْرِيمِ: ٨] . فَلَا يَذْكُرُ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ أَحَدٌ أَحَدًا" وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَضُرِبَ بَيْنَهُمْ بِسُورٍ لَهُ بَابٌ بَاطِنُهُ فِيهِ الرَّحْمَةُ وَظَاهِرُهُ مِنْ قِبَلِهِ الْعَذَابُ﴾ قَالَ الْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ: هُوَ حَائِطٌ بَيْنَ الْجَنَّةِ النَّارِ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: هُوَ الَّذِي قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَبَيْنَهُمَا حِجَابٌ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٤٦] . وَهَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ، وَهُوَ الصَّحِيحُ.

﴿بَاطِنُهُ فِيهِ الرَّحْمَةُ﴾ أَيِ: الْجَنَّةُ وَمَا فِيهَا ﴿وَظَاهِرُهُ مِنْ قِبَلِهِ الْعَذَابُ﴾ أَيِ: النَّارُ. قَالَهُ قتادة، وبن زيد، وغيرهما.

قال بن جَرِيرٍ: وَقَدْ قِيلَ: إِنَّ ذَلِكَ السُّورَ سورُ بَيْتِ الْمَقْدِسِ عِنْدَ وَادِي جَهَنَّمَ. ثُمَّ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ الْبَرْقِيِّ، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ عَطِيَّةَ بْنِ قَيْسٍ، عن أبي العوام- مُؤَذِّنِ بَيْتِ الْمَقْدِسِ-قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عَمْرٍو يَقُولُ: إِنَّ السُّورَ الَّذِي ذَكَرَ اللَّهُ فِي الْقُرْآنِ: ﴿فَضُرِبَ بَيْنَهُمْ بِسُورٍ لَهُ بَابٌ بَاطِنُهُ فِيهِ الرَّحْمَةُ وَظَاهِرُهُ مِنْ قِبَلِهِ الْعَذَابُ﴾ هُوَ السُّورُ الشَّرْقِيُّ بَاطِنُهُ الْمَسْجِدُ وَمَا يَلِيهِ، وَظَاهِرُهُ وَادِي جَهَنَّمَ.

ثُمَّ رُوِيَ عَنْ عُبَادَةَ بْنِ الصَّامِتِ، وَكَعْبِ الْأَحْبَارِ، وَعَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ زَيْنِ الْعَابِدِينَ، نَحْوُ ذَلِكَ. وَهَذَا مَحْمُولٌ مِنْهُمْ عَلَى أَنَّهُمْ أَرَادُوا بِهَذَا تَقْرِيبَ الْمَعْنَى وَمِثَالًا لِذَلِكَ، لَا أَنَّ هَذَا هُوَ الَّذِي أُرِيدَ مِنَ الْقُرْآنِ هَذَا الْجِدَارُ الْمُعَيَّنُ وَنَفْسُ الْمَسْجِدِ وَمَا وَرَاءَهُ مِنَ الْوَادِي الْمَعْرُوفِ بِوَادِي جهنم؛ فإن الجنة في السموات فِي أَعْلَى عِلِّيِّينَ، وَالنَّارَ فِي الدَّرَكَاتِ أَسْفَلَ سَافِلِينَ. وَقَوْلُ كَعْبِ الْأَحْبَارِ: إِنَّ الْبَابَ الْمَذْكُورَ فِي الْقُرْآنِ هُوَ بَابُ الرَّحْمَةِ الَّذِي هُوَ أَحَدُ أَبْوَابِ الْمَسْجِدِ، فَهَذَا مِنْ إِسْرَائِيلِيَّاتِهِ وتُرّهاته. وَإِنَّمَا الْمُرَادُ بِذَلِكَ: سورٌ يُضْرَب يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ لِيَحْجِزَ بَيْنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ وَالْمُنَافِقِينَ، فَإِذَا انْتَهَى إِلَيْهِ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ دَخَلُوهُ مِنْ بَابِهِ، فَإِذَا اسْتَكْمَلُوا دُخولهم أُغْلِقَ الْبَابُ وَبَقِيَ الْمُنَافِقُونَ مِنْ وَرَائِهِ فِي الْحَيْرَةِ وَالظُّلْمَةِ وَالْعَذَابِ، كَمَا كَانُوا فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا فِي كَفْرٍ وَجَهْلٍ وَشَكٍّ وَحَيْرَةٍ ﴿يُنَادُونَهُمْ أَلَمْ نَكُنْ مَعَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: يُنَادِي الْمُنَافِقُونَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ: أَمَا كُنَّا مَعَكُمْ فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا، نَشْهَدُ مَعَكُمُ الْجُمُعَاتِ، وَنُصَلِّي مَعَكُمُ الْجَمَاعَاتِ، وَنَقِفُ مَعَكُمْ بِعَرَفَاتٍ، وَنَحْضُرُ مَعَكُمُ الْغَزَوَاتِ، وَنُؤَدِّي مَعَكُمْ سَائِرَ الْوَاجِبَاتِ؟ ﴿قَالُوا بَلَى﴾ أَيْ: فَأَجَابَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ قَائِلِينَ: بَلَى، قَدْ كُنْتُمْ مَعَنَا، ﴿وَلَكِنَّكُمْ فَتَنْتُمْ أَنْفُسَكُمْ وَتَرَبَّصْتُمْ وَارْتَبْتُمْ وَغَرَّتْكُمُ الأمَانِيُّ﴾ قَالَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ: أَيْ فَتَنْتُمْ أَنْفُسَكُمْ بِاللَّذَّاتِ وَالْمَعَاصِي وَالشَّهَوَاتِ ﴿وَتَرَبَّصْتُمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَخَّرْتُمُ التَّوْبَةَ مِنْ وَقْتٍ إِلَى وَقْتٍ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿وَتَرَبَّصْتُمْ﴾ بِالْحَقِّ وَأَهْلِهِ ﴿وَارْتَبْتُمْ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْبَعْثِ بَعْدَ الْمَوْتِ ﴿وَغَرَّتْكُمُ الأمَانِيُّ﴾ أَيْ: قُلْتُمْ: سَيُغْفَرُ لَنَا. وَقِيلَ: غَرَّتْكُمُ الدُّنْيَا ﴿حَتَّى جَاءَ أَمْرُ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: مَا زِلْتُمْ فِي هَذَا حَتَّى جَاءَ الْمَوْتُ ﴿وَغَرَّكُمْ بِاللَّهِ الْغَرُورُ﴾ أَيِ: الشَّيْطَانُ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: كَانُوا عَلَى خَدْعَةٍ مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ، وَاللَّهِ مَا زَالُوا عَلَيْهَا حَتَّى قَذَفَهُمُ اللَّهُ فِي النَّارِ.

وَمَعْنَى هَذَا الْكَلَامِ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ لِلْمُنَافِقِينَ: إِنَّكُمْ كُنْتُمْ مَعَنَا [أَيْ] بِأَبْدَانٍ لَا نِيَّةَ لَهَا وَلَا قُلُوبَ مَعَهَا، وإنما كنتم في حيرة وشك فكنتم تُراؤون النَّاسَ وَلَا تَذْكُرُونَ اللَّهَ إِلَّا قَلِيلًا.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: كَانَ الْمُنَافِقُونَ مَعَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَحْيَاءً يُنَاكِحُونَهُمْ وَيَغُشُّونَهُمْ وَيُعَاشِرُونَهُمْ، وَكَانُوا مَعَهُمْ أَمْوَاتًا، وَيُعْطَوْنَ النُّورَ جَمِيعًا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَيُطْفَأُ النُّورُ مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ إِذَا بَلَغُوا السُّورَ، ويُماز بَيْنَهُمْ حِينَئِذٍ.

وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ لَا يُنَافِي قَوْلَهُمُ الَّذِي أَخْبَرَ اللَّهُ بِهِ عَنْهُمْ، حَيْثُ يَقُولُ-وَهُوَ أَصْدَقُ الْقَائِلِينَ-: ﴿كُلُّ نَفْسٍ بِمَا كَسَبَتْ رَهِينَةٌ إِلا أَصْحَابَ الْيَمِينِ فِي جَنَّاتٍ يَتَسَاءَلُونَ عَنِ الْمُجْرِمِينَ مَا سَلَكَكُمْ فِي سَقَرَ قَالُوا لَمْ نَكُ مِنَ الْمُصَلِّينَ وَلَمْ نَكُ نُطْعِمُ الْمِسْكِينَ وَكُنَّا نَخُوضُ مَعَ الْخَائِضِينَ وَكُنَّا نُكَذِّبُ بِيَوْمِ الدِّينِ حَتَّى أَتَانَا الْيَقِينُ﴾ [الْمُدَّثِّرِ: ٣٨-٤٧] ، فَهَذَا إِنَّمَا خَرَجَ مِنْهُمْ عَلَى وَجْهِ التَّقْرِيعِ لَهُمْ وَالتَّوْبِيخِ. ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَمَا تَنْفَعُهُمْ شَفَاعَةُ الشَّافِعِينَ﴾ [المدثر: ٤٨] ، كما قال تعالى هاهنا: ﴿فَالْيَوْمَ لَا يُؤْخَذُ مِنْكُمْ فِدْيَةٌ وَلا مِنَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا﴾ أَيْ: لَوْ جَاءَ أَحَدُكُمُ الْيَوْمَ بِمِلْءِ الْأَرْضِ ذَهَبًا وَمِثْلِهِ مَعَهُ لِيَفْتَدِيَ بِهِ مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ، مَا قُبِلَ مِنْهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَأْوَاكُمُ النَّارُ﴾ أَيْ: هِيَ مَصِيرُكُمْ وَإِلَيْهَا مُنْقَلَبُكُمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿هِيَ مَوْلاكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: هِيَ أَوْلَى بِكُمْ مِنْ كُلِّ مَنْزِلٍ عَلَى كُفْرِكُمْ وَارْتِيَابِكُمْ، وَبِئْسَ الْمَصِيرُ.

---

## 57:16-17 — verses 16-17 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah, exalted is He, says: has the time not come for the believers that their hearts should be humbled at the remembrance of Allah, that is, that they should soften at the reminder, the exhortation, and the hearing of the Qur'an, so that they understand it, submit to it, listen to it, and obey it.

Abdullah ibn al-Mubarak said: Salih al-Murri narrated to us, from Qatadah, from Ibn Abbas, that he said: Allah found the hearts of the Muhajirun slow, and so He rebuked them at the head of the thirteenth year from the revelation of the Qur'an, saying: {Has the time not come for those who believe that their hearts should be humbled at the remembrance of Allah} the verse. Ibn Abi Hatim narrated this, from al-Hasan ibn Muhammad ibn al-Sabbah, from Husayn al-Marwazi, from Ibn al-Mubarak, with this chain.

Then he, along with Muslim, said: [chain] Yunus ibn Abd al-A'la narrated to us, Ibn Wahb informed us, Amr ibn al-Harith informed me, from Sa'id ibn Abi Hilal, that is al-Layth, from Awn ibn Abdullah, from his father, from Ibn Mas'ud, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: between our accepting Islam and Allah's rebuking us with this verse, {Has the time not come for those who believe that their hearts should be humbled at the remembrance of Allah} the verse, there was only four years.

This is how Muslim narrated it at the end of the book. Al-Nasa'i also transmitted it in his commentary on this verse, from Harun ibn Sa'id al-Ayli, from Ibn Wahb, with this chain. Ibn Majah narrated it from the hadith of Musa ibn Ya'qub al-Zam'i, from Abu Hazm, from Amir ibn Abdullah ibn al-Zubayr, from his father, in similar wording, making it part of the musnad of Ibn al-Zubayr. However, al-Bazzar narrated it in his Musnad through the route of Musa ibn Ya'qub, from Abu Hazim, from Amir, from Ibn al-Zubayr, from Ibn Mas'ud, and mentioned it thus.

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from al-Mas'udi, from al-Qasim, who said: the companions of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ grew weary at one point, and said, "Narrate to us, O Messenger of Allah." So Allah, exalted is He, revealed: {We relate to you the best of narrations} [Yusuf: 3]. He said: then they grew weary again and said, "Narrate to us, O Messenger of Allah." So Allah, exalted is He, revealed: {Allah has sent down the best of speech} [al-Zumar: 23]. Then they grew weary again and said, "Narrate to us, O Messenger of Allah." So Allah revealed: {Has the time not come for those who believe that their hearts should be humbled at the remembrance of Allah}.

Qatadah said, regarding {Has the time not come for those who believe that their hearts should be humbled at the remembrance of Allah}: it was mentioned to us that Shaddad ibn Aws used to narrate from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ that he said: "The first thing to be lifted from among the people is khushu' (humble submissiveness)."

Concerning His saying: {And that they not be like those who were given the Scripture before, and time grew long for them, so their hearts hardened}, Allah forbade the believers from resembling those who bore the Scripture before them, the Jews and the Christians, who, when time grew long upon them, altered the Book of Allah that was in their hands, sold it for a small price, cast it behind their backs, turned to differing opinions and false statements, followed men blindly in matters of Allah's religion, and took their rabbis and monks as lords besides Allah. At that point their hearts hardened, so that they would not accept exhortation, and their hearts would not soften at either promise or warning.

{And many of them are defiantly disobedient} that is, in their deeds, for their hearts were corrupt and their works void. As He said: {So for their breaking of their covenant, We cursed them and made their hearts hard. They distort words from their places and have forgotten a portion of what they were reminded of} [al-Ma'idah: 13], that is, their hearts became corrupted and hardened, and it became their nature to distort words from their places; they abandoned the deeds they had been commanded to do, and committed what they had been forbidden from. For this reason Allah forbade the believers from resembling them in anything, whether in matters of fundamental principle or in secondary matters.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] my father narrated to us, Hisham ibn Ammar narrated to us, Shihab ibn Khirash narrated to us, Hajjaj ibn Dinar narrated to us, from Mansur ibn al-Mu'tamir, from al-Rabi' ibn Abi Amilah al-Fazari, who said: Abdullah ibn Mas'ud narrated to us a hadith than which I have heard nothing more astonishing to me, except something from the Book of Allah, or something the Prophet ﷺ said. He said: "When time grew long upon the Children of Israel and their hearts hardened, they fabricated a book from among themselves, which their hearts found appealing, which their tongues found permissible, and which they found delightful, whereas the truth used to stand between them and many of their desires. So they said: let us call the Children of Israel to this book of ours; whoever follows us in it, we shall leave him be, and whoever refuses to follow us, we shall kill him. So they did that. Among them was a learned man, and when he saw what they were doing, he took what he knew of the Book of Allah and wrote it on something small, then rolled it up and placed it inside a horn, then hung that horn around his neck. When they had killed many, some of them said to others: O people, you have spread killing widely among the Children of Israel; so summon so-and-so and present your book to him, for if he follows you, the rest of the people will follow you, and if he refuses, kill him. So they summoned that learned man and said: do you believe in what is in our book? He said: what is in it? Show it to me. So they presented it to him to its end, then said: do you believe in this? He said: yes, I believe in what is in this, and he pointed with his hand to the horn, so they left him be. When he died, they dug up his grave and found the horn still hanging on him, and found in it what he knew of the Book of Allah. So some of them said to others: O people, we never used to hear this, some trial must have befallen him. So the Children of Israel split into seventy-two sects, and the best of their sects is the sect of the companions of the horn."

Ibn Mas'ud said: "And indeed it is close for you, if you remain, or if those of you who remain do remain, that you will see matters that you will disapprove of, yet be unable to change. So it is enough for a man among you that Allah know from his heart that he detests it."

Abu Ja'far al-Tabari said: [chain] Ibn Humayd narrated to us, Jarir narrated to us, from Mughirah, from Abu Ma'shar, from Ibrahim, who said: Atris ibn Urqub came to Ibn Mas'ud and said: O Abu Abdullah, whoever does not enjoin what is right and forbid what is wrong has perished. Abdullah said: whoever's heart does not recognize what is right and whose heart does not disapprove of what is wrong has perished. Indeed, when time grew long upon the Children of Israel and their hearts hardened, they fabricated a book from between their own hands and feet, which their hearts found appealing and which their tongues found permissible, and they said: we shall present this book to the Children of Israel, and whoever believes in it we shall leave be, and whoever disbelieves in it we shall kill. He said: so a man among them put the Book of Allah into a horn, then placed the horn between his two breasts. When it was said to him, "Do you believe in this?" he said, "I believe in it," gesturing toward the horn between his two breasts, "and why should I not believe in this book?" So the best of their sects today is the sect of the companion of the horn.

Concerning His saying: {Know that Allah gives life to the earth after its death. We have made clear to you the signs, that you might understand}, there is in this an indication that He, exalted is He, softens hearts after their hardness, guides the bewildered after their straying, and relieves distresses after their intensity. Just as He gives life to the dead, barren, still earth with abundant, pouring rain, so too does He guide hardened hearts by the proofs and evidences of the Qur'an, and He causes light to enter them after they had been locked, unreachable by any who might reach them. So glory be to Him who guides whomever He wills after leading astray, and who leads astray whomever He intends after completeness, He who does whatever He wills, and who is the just Arbiter in all deeds, the Subtle, the All-Aware, the Most Great, the Most Exalted.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: أَمَا آنَ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَنْ تَخْشَعَ قُلُوبُهُمْ لِذِكْرِ اللَّهِ، أَيْ: تَلِينَ عِنْدَ الذِّكْرِ وَالْمَوْعِظَةِ وَسَمَاعِ الْقُرْآنِ، فَتَفْهَمَهُ وتنقادُ لَهُ وَتَسْمَعَ لَهُ وَتُطِيعَهُ.

قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ: حَدَّثَنَا صَالِحٍ المُرِّي، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ اسْتَبْطَأَ قُلُوبَ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ فَعَاتَبَهُمْ عَلَى رَأْسِ ثَلَاثَ عَشْرَةَ مِنْ نُزُولِ الْقُرْآنِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿أَلَمْ يَأْنِ لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَنْ تَخْشَعَ قُلُوبُهُمْ لِذِكْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ الْآيَةَ، رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ الصَّبَّاحِ، عَنْ حُسَيْنٍ الْمَرْوَزِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ الْمُبَارَكِ، بِهِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ هُوَ وَمُسْلِمٌ: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْأَعْلَى، أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي عَمْرُو بْنُ الْحَارِثِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي هِلَالٍ-يَعْنِي اللَّيْثَ-عَنْ عَوْنِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: مَا كَانَ بَيْنَ إِسْلَامِنَا وَبَيْنَ أَنْ عَاتَبَنَا اللَّهُ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ ﴿أَلَمْ يَأْنِ لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَنْ تَخْشَعَ قُلُوبُهُمْ لِذِكْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ [الْآيَةَ] إِلَّا أَرْبَعُ سِنِينَ 

كَذَا رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ فِي آخِرِ الْكِتَابِ. وَأَخْرَجَهُ النَّسَائِيُّ عِنْدَ تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ، عَنْ هَارُونَ بْنِ سَعِيدٍ الْأَيْلِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ وَهْبٍ، بِهِ وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُوسَى بْنِ يَعْقُوبَ الزَّمْعِيِّ عَنْ أَبِي حَزْمٍ، عَنْ عَامِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، مِثْلَهُ فَجَعَلَهُ مِنْ مُسْنَدِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ. لَكِنْ رَوَاهُ الْبَزَّارُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ مِنْ طَرِيقِ مُوسَى بْنِ يَعْقُوبَ، عَنْ أَبِي حَازِمٍ، عَنْ عامر، عن بن الزبير، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، فَذَكَرَهُ 

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنِ الْمَسْعُودِيِّ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ قَالَ: مَلَّ أَصْحَابُ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَلَّةً، فقالوا: حدثنا يا رسول الله. فأنزل الله تَعَالَى: ﴿نَحْنُ نَقُصُّ عَلَيْكَ أَحْسَنَ الْقَصَصِ﴾ [يُوسُفَ:٣] قَالَ: ثُمَّ مَلُّوا مَلَّةً فَقَالُوا: حَدِّثْنَا يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿اللَّهُ نزلَ أَحْسَنَ الْحَدِيثِ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ:٢٣] . ثُمَّ مَلُّوا مَلَّةً فَقَالُوا: حَدِّثْنَا يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ. فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿أَلَمْ يَأْنِ لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَنْ تَخْشَعَ قُلُوبُهُمْ لِذِكْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ 

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿أَلَمْ يَأْنِ لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَنْ تَخْشَعَ قُلُوبُهُمْ لِذِكْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ ذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ شَدَّادَ بْنَ أَوْسٍ كَانَ يَرْوِي عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قال: "إِنَّ أَوَّلَ مَا يُرْفَعُ مِنَ النَّاسِ الْخُشُوعُ" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا يَكُونُوا كَالَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ مِنْ قَبْلُ فَطَالَ عَلَيْهِمُ الأمَدُ فَقَسَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ﴾ نَهَى اللَّهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَنْ يَتَشَبَّهُوا بِالَّذِينِ حَمَلُوا الْكِتَابَ قَبْلَهُمْ مِنَ الْيَهُودِ وَالنَّصَارَى، لَمَّا تَطَاوَلَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْأَمَدُ بَدَّلُوا كِتَابَ اللَّهِ الَّذِي بِأَيْدِيهمْ وَاشْتَرَوْا بِهِ ثَمَنًا قَلِيلًا وَنَبَذُوهُ وَرَاءَ ظُهُورِهِمْ، وَأَقْبَلُوا عَلَى الْآرَاءِ الْمُخْتَلِفَةِ وَالْأَقْوَالِ الْمُؤْتَفِكَةِ، وَقَلَّدُوا الرِّجَالَ فِي دِينِ اللَّهِ، وَاتَّخَذُوا أَحْبَارَهُمْ وَرُهْبَانَهُمْ أَرْبَابًا مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ، فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ قَسَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ، فَلَا يَقْبَلُونَ مَوْعِظَةً، وَلَا تَلِينُ قُلُوبُهُمْ بِوَعْدٍ وَلَا وَعِيدٍ.

﴿وَكَثِيرٌ مِنْهُمْ فَاسِقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الْأَعْمَالِ، فَقُلُوبُهُمْ فَاسِدَةٌ، وَأَعْمَالُهُمْ بَاطِلَةٌ. كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿فَبِمَا نَقْضِهِمْ مِيثَاقَهُمْ لَعَنَّاهُمْ وَجَعَلْنَا قُلُوبَهُمْ قَاسِيَةً يُحَرِّفُونَ الْكَلِمَ عَنْ مَوَاضِعِهِ وَنَسُوا حَظًّا مِمَّا ذُكِّرُوا بِهِ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ:١٣] ، أَيْ: فَسَدَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ فَقَسَتْ وَصَارَ مِنْ سَجِيَّتِهِمْ تَحْرِيفُ الْكَلِمِ عَنْ مَوَاضِعِهِ، وَتَرَكُوا الْأَعْمَالَ الَّتِي أُمِرُوا بِهَا، وَارْتَكَبُوا مَا نهو عَنْهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا نَهَى اللَّهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَنْ يَتَشَبَّهُوا بِهِمْ فِي شَيْءٍ مِنَ الْأُمُورِ الْأَصْلِيَّةِ وَالْفَرْعِيَّةِ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ بْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ عَمَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شِهَابُ بْنُ خِراش، حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجُ بْنُ دِينَارٍ، عَنْ مَنْصُورِ بْنِ الْمُعْتَمِرِ، عَنِ الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ أَبِي عَمِيلة الْفَزَارِيِّ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مَسْعُودٍ حَدِيثًا مَا سَمِعْتُ أَعْجَبَ إليَّ مِنْهُ، إِلَّا شَيْئًا مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ-أَوْ: شَيْئًا قَالَهُ النبي صلى الله عليه وسلم-قال: "إن بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ لَمَّا طَالَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْأَمَدُ فَقَسَتْ قُلُوبُهُمُ اخْتَرَعُوا كِتَابًا مِنْ عِنْدِ أَنْفُسِهِمْ، اسْتَهْوَتْهُ قُلُوبُهُمْ وَاسْتَحَلَّتْهُ أَلْسِنَتُهُمْ وَاسْتَلَذَّتْهُ، وَكَانَ الْحَقُّ يَحُولُ بَيْنَهُمْ وَبَيْنَ كَثِيرٍ مِنْ شَهَوَاتِهِمْ فَقَالُوا: تَعَالَوْا ندع بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ إِلَى كِتَابِنَا هَذَا، فَمَنْ تَابَعَنَا عَلَيْهِ تَرَكْنَاهُ، وَمَنْ كَرِهَ أَنْ يُتَابِعَنَا قَتَلْنَاهُ. فَفَعَلُوا ذَلِكَ، وَكَانَ فِيهِمْ رِجُلٌ فَقِيهٌ، فَلَمَّا رَأَى مَا يَصْنَعُونَ عَمَدَ إِلَى مَا يَعْرِفُ مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ فَكَتَبَهُ فِي شَيْءٍ لَطِيفٍ، ثُمَّ أَدْرَجَهُ، فَجَعَلَهُ فِي قَرْنٍ ثُمَّ عَلَّقَ ذَلِكَ الْقَرْنَ فِي عُنُقِهِ، فَلَمَّا أَكْثَرُوا الْقَتْلَ قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ: يَا هَؤُلَاءِ، إِنَّكُمْ قَدْ أَفْشَيْتُمُ الْقَتْلَ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَادْعُوا فُلَانًا فَاعْرِضُوا عَلَيْهِ كِتَابَكُمْ، فَإِنَّهُ إِنْ تَابَعَكُمْ فَسَيُتَابِعُكُمْ بَقِيَّةُ النَّاسِ، وَإِنْ أَبَى فَاقْتُلُوهُ. فَدَعَوْا فُلَانًا ذَلِكَ الْفَقِيهَ فَقَالُوا: تُؤْمِنُ بِمَا فِي كِتَابِنَا؟ قَالَ: وَمَا فِيهِ؟ اعْرِضُوهُ عليَّ. فَعَرَضُوهُ عَلَيْهِ إِلَى آخِرِهِ، ثُمَّ قَالُوا: أَتُؤْمِنُ بِهَذَا؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ، آمَنْتُ بِمَا فِي هَذَا وَأَشَارَ بِيَدِهِ إِلَى الْقَرْنِ-فَتَرَكُوهُ، فَلَمَّا مَاتَ نَبَشُوهُ فَوَجَدُوهُ مُتَعَلِّقًا ذَلِكَ الْقَرْنَ، فَوَجَدُوا فِيهِ مَا يَعْرِفُ مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ، فَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ: يَا هَؤُلَاءِ، مَا كُنَّا نَسْمَعُ هَذَا أَصَابَهُ فِتْنَةٌ. فَافْتَرَقَتْ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ عَلَى ثِنْتَيْنِ وَسَبْعِينَ مِلَّةً، وَخَيْرُ ملَلهم مِلَّةُ أَصْحَابِ ذِي الْقَرْنِ".

قَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: [وَإِنَّكُمْ] أَوْشَكَ بِكُمْ إِنْ بَقِيتُمْ-أَوْ: بَقِيَ مَنْ بَقِيَ مِنْكُمْ -أَنْ تَرَوْا أُمُورًا تُنْكِرُونَهَا، لَا تَسْتَطِيعُونَ لَهَا غِيَرًا، فَبِحَسْبِ الْمَرْءِ مِنْكُمْ أَنْ يَعْلَمَ اللَّهُ مِنْ قَلْبِهِ أَنَّهُ لَهَا كَارِهٌ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الطَّبَرِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حُمَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرٌ، عَنْ مُغِيرَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي مَعْشَرٍ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ قَالَ: جَاءَ عتريس بن عُرقوب إلى بن مَسْعُودٍ فَقَالَ: يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ اللَّهِ هَلَكَ من لم يأمر بالمعروف وينهى عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ. فَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ: هَلَكَ مَنْ لَمْ يَعْرِفْ قلبُه مَعْرُوفًا وَلَمْ يُنْكِرْ قلبُه مُنْكَرًا؛ إِنَّ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ لَمَّا طَالَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْأَمَدُ وَقَسَتْ قُلُوبُهُمُ، اخْتَرَعُوا كِتَابًا مِنْ بَيْنِ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَأَرْجُلِهِمُ، اسْتَهْوَتْهُ قُلُوبُهُمْ وَاسْتَحَلَّتْهُ أَلْسِنَتُهُمْ، وَقَالُوا: نَعْرِضُ عَلَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ هَذَا الْكِتَابَ فَمَنْ آمَنَ بِهِ تَرَكْنَاهُ، وَمَنْ كَفَرَ بِهِ قَتَلْنَاهُ. قَالَ: فَجَعَلَ رَجُلٌ مِنْهُمْ كِتَابَ اللَّهِ فِي قَرْن، ثُمَّ جَعَلَ الْقَرْنَ بَيْنَ ثَنْدُوَتَيْهِ فَلَمَّا قِيلَ لَهُ: أَتُؤْمِنُ بِهَذَا؟ قَالَ آمَنْتُ بِهِ -وَيُومِئُ إِلَى الْقَرْنِ بَيْنَ ثَنْدُوتيه-وَمَالِي لَا أُؤْمِنُ بِهَذَا الْكِتَابِ؟ فَمِنْ خَيْرِ مِلَلِهم الْيَوْمَ مِلَّة صَاحِبِ القَرن 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿اعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ يُحْيِي الأرْضَ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا قَدْ بَيَّنَّا لَكُمُ الآيَاتِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَعْقِلُونَ﴾ فِيهِ إِشَارَةٌ إِلَى أَنَّهُ، تَعَالَى، يُلِينُ الْقُلُوبَ بَعْدَ قَسْوَتِهَا، ويَهدي الحَيَارى بَعْدَ ضَلتها، ويفرِّج الْكُرُوبَ بَعْدَ شِدَّتِهَا، فَكَمَا يُحْيِي الْأَرْضَ الْمَيِّتَةَ الْمُجْدِبَةَ الْهَامِدَةَ بِالْغَيْثِ الهتَّان [الْوَابِلِ] كَذَلِكَ يَهْدِي الْقُلُوبَ الْقَاسِيَةَ بِبَرَاهِينِ الْقُرْآنِ وَالدَّلَائِلِ، وَيُولِجُ إِلَيْهَا النُّورَ بَعْدَ مَا كَانَتْ مُقْفَلَةً لَا يَصِلُ إِلَيْهَا الْوَاصِلُ، فَسُبْحَانَ الْهَادِي لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ بَعْدَ الْإِضْلَالِ، وَالْمُضِلِّ لِمَنْ أَرَادَ بَعْدَ الْكَمَالِ، الَّذِي هُوَ لِمَا يَشَاءُ فَعَّالٌ، وَهُوَ الْحَكَمُ الْعَدْلُ فِي جَمِيعِ الْفِعَالِ، اللَّطِيفُ الخبير الكبير المتعال.

---

## 57:18-19 — verses 18-19 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs about what He will reward those men and women who give charity from their wealth to people in need, poverty, and destitution. {And have lent to Allah a goodly loan} means: they gave it with a sincere intention, seeking the face of Allah, not wanting any repayment or thanks from those they gave to. Therefore He said: {it will be multiplied for them}, meaning He will match their good deed with ten times its like, and increase beyond that up to seven hundred fold and beyond. {And theirs is a noble reward} meaning an abundant, excellent reward, and a good return and a {noble} homecoming.

His saying: {And those who believe in Allah and His messengers, those are the truthful ones (al-siddiqun)} completes the description of those who believe in Allah and His messengers, stating that they are truthful ones.

Al-'Awfi said, from Ibn 'Abbas, regarding His saying: {And those who believe in Allah and His messengers, those are the truthful ones}, that this is a separate statement, and {the martyrs, with their Lord, they have their reward and their light} is separate as well.

Abu al-Duha said: {those are the truthful ones}, then the speech begins anew, saying: {and the martyrs, with their Lord}. Masruq, al-Dahhak, Muqatil ibn Hayyan, and others said likewise.

Al-A'mash reported from Abu al-Duha, from Masruq, from 'Abdullah, regarding His saying: {those are the truthful ones and the martyrs, with their Lord}, that he said: They are three categories, meaning: those who give charity (al-musaddiqin), the truthful ones (al-siddiqin), and the martyrs (al-shuhada'), just as Allah, the Exalted, said: {And whoever obeys Allah and the Messenger, those will be with those whom Allah has favored: the prophets, the truthful, the martyrs, and the righteous} [al-Nisa': 69]. He distinguished between the truthful and the martyrs, indicating that they are two distinct categories. There is no doubt that the truthful one holds a higher station than the martyr, as related by Imam Malik ibn Anas, may Allah have mercy on him, in his book al-Muwatta, from Safwan ibn Sulaym, from 'Ata' ibn Yasar, from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The people of Paradise will look up at the people of the elevated chambers above them just as you look at a radiant star remaining in the horizon in the east or the west, due to the difference in rank between them." They said: "O Messenger of Allah, are those the dwellings of the prophets, which none but they can reach?" He said: "Certainly not, by the One in whose hand is my soul, they are men who believed in Allah and affirmed the truth of the messengers."

Both al-Bukhari and Muslim agreed in extracting this from the hadith of Malik, with this chain.

Others said: rather, what is meant by His saying, {those are the truthful ones and the martyrs, with their Lord}, is that He is informing about the believers in Allah and His messengers, that they are both truthful ones and martyrs. Ibn Jarir related this from Mujahid. Ibn Jarir then said: [chain] al-Bara' ibn 'Azib said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "The believers of my nation are martyrs." He said: then the Prophet ﷺ recited this verse: {And those who believe in Allah and His messengers, those are the truthful ones and the martyrs, with their Lord, they have their reward}. This is a gharib (singular) hadith.

Abu Ishaq said, from 'Amr ibn Maymun, regarding His saying: {And those who believe in Allah and His messengers, those are the truthful ones and the martyrs, with their Lord, they have their reward and their light}, that he said: They will come on the Day of Resurrection together, like two fingers side by side.

His saying: {and the martyrs, with their Lord} means: in the gardens of bliss, as has come in the two Sahihs: "The spirits of the martyrs are in the crops of green birds that roam freely in Paradise wherever they wish, then they take shelter in those lamps. Your Lord looked upon them with a glance and said: 'What do you wish for?' They said: 'We wish that You return us to the worldly abode so that we may fight for Your sake and be killed as we were killed the first time.' He said: 'I have decreed that they shall not return to it.'"

His saying: {they have their reward and their light} means: with their Lord they have an abundant reward and a great light that moves before them, and in this they differ in degree according to what deeds they performed in the worldly life, as Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Fadala ibn 'Ubayd said: I heard 'Umar ibn al-Khattab say: I heard the Prophet ﷺ say: "The martyrs are of four kinds: a believing man of sound faith who meets the enemy, is truthful with Allah, and is killed. That is the one whom people will look at like this," and he raised his head until the cap of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, or the cap of 'Umar, fell off, "and the second is a believer who meets the enemy as though his back were being struck with thorns of the acacia tree, a stray arrow comes to him and kills him. That one is in the second rank. The third is a believing man who mixed a righteous deed with another that was evil, who meets the enemy and is truthful with Allah until he is killed. That one is in the third rank. And the fourth is a believing man who wronged himself greatly, who meets the enemy and is truthful with Allah until he is killed. That one is in the fourth rank."

Thus it was related by 'Ali ibn al-Madini, from Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi, from Ibn al-Mubarak, from Ibn Lahi'a, who said: This is a sound Egyptian chain. Al-Tirmidhi related it from the hadith of Ibn Lahi'a and said: hasan gharib.

His saying: {And those who disbelieved and denied Our signs, those are the companions of the Blazing Fire}: having mentioned the fortunate ones and their final outcome, He follows with mention of the wretched ones and clarifies their condition.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَمَّا يُثِيبُ بِهِ المُصَّدقين والمُصَّدقات بِأَمْوَالِهِمْ عَلَى أَهْلِ الْحَاجَةِ وَالْفَقْرِ وَالْمَسْكَنَةِ، ﴿وَأَقْرَضُوا اللَّهَ قَرْضًا حَسَنًا﴾ أَيْ: دَفَعُوهُ بِنِيَّةٍ خَالِصَةٍ ابْتِغَاءَ وَجْهِ اللَّهِ، لَا يُرِيدُونَ جَزَاءً مِمَّنْ أَعْطَوْهُ وَلَا شُكُورًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿يُضَاعَفُ لَهُمُ﴾ أَيْ: يُقَابِلُ لَهُمُ الْحَسَنَةَ بِعَشْرِ أَمْثَالِهَا، وَيَزْدَادُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ إِلَى سَبْعِمِائَةِ ضِعْفٍ وَفَوْقَ ذَلِكَ ﴿وَلَهُمْ أَجْرٌ كَرِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: ثَوَابٌ جَزِيلٌ حَسَنٌ، وَمَرْجِعٌ صَالِحٌ وَمَآبٌ ﴿كَرِيمٌ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الصِّدِّيقُونَ﴾ هَذَا تَمَامٌ لِجُمْلَةِ، وَصْفِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ بِأَنَّهُمْ صِدِّيقُونَ.

قَالَ العَوْفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الصِّدِّيقُونَ﴾ هَذِهِ مَفْصُولَةٌ ﴿وَالشُّهَدَاءُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ لَهُمْ أَجْرُهُمْ وَنُورُهُمْ﴾ .

وَقَالَ أَبُو الضُّحَى: ﴿أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الصِّدِّيقُونَ﴾ ثُمَّ اسْتَأْنَفَ الْكَلَامَ فَقَالَ: ﴿وَالشُّهَدَاءُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ﴾ وَهَكَذَا قَالَ مَسْرُوقٌ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَمُقَاتِلُ بْنُ حَيَّانَ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ عَنْ أَبِي الضُّحَى، عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الصِّدِّيقُونَ وَالشُّهَدَاءُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ﴾ قَالَ: هُمْ ثَلَاثَةُ أَصْنَافٍ: يَعْنِي الْمُصَدِّقِينَ، وَالصِّدِّيقِينَ، وَالشُّهَدَاءَ، كَمَا قَالَ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَنْ يُطِعِ اللَّهَ وَالرَّسُولَ فَأُولَئِكَ مَعَ الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنَ النَّبِيِّينَ وَالصِّدِّيقِينَ وَالشُّهَدَاءِ وَالصَّالِحِينَ﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ٦٩] فَفَرَّقَ بَيْنَ الصِّدِّيقِينَ وَالشُّهَدَاءِ، فَدَلَّ عَلَى أَنَّهُمَا صِنْفَانِ. وَلَا شَكَّ أَنَّ الصِّدِّيقَ أَعْلَى مَقَامًا مِنَ الشَّهِيدِ، كَمَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ مَالِكُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، فِي كِتَابِهِ الْمُوَطَّإِ، عَنْ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ سُلَيْمٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَار، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ لَيَتَرَاءَوْنَ أَهْلَ الْغُرَفِ مِنْ فَوْقِهِمْ، كَمَا تَتَرَاءَوْنَ الْكَوْكَبَ الدُّرِّيَّ الْغَابِرَ فِي الْأُفُقِ مِنَ الْمَشْرِقِ أَوِ الْمَغْرِبِ، لِتَفَاضُلِ مَا بَيْنَهُمْ". قَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، تِلْكَ مَنَازِلُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ لَا يَبْلُغُهَا غَيْرُهُمْ؟ قَالَ: "بَلَى وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، رِجَالٌ آمَنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَصَدَّقُوا الْمُرْسَلِينَ".

اتَّفَقَ الْبُخَارِيُّ وَمُسْلِمٌ عَلَى إِخْرَاجِهِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ مَالِكٍ، بِهِ 

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: بَلِ الْمُرَادُ مِنْ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الصِّدِّيقُونَ وَالشُّهَدَاءُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ﴾ فَأَخْبَرَ عَنِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ بِأَنَّهُمْ صِدِّيقُونَ وَشُهَدَاءُ. حَكَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنْ مجاهد، ثم قال ابن جرير: حدثني صالح ابن حَرْبٍ أَبُو مَعْمَر، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ يَحْيَى، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنِ عَجْلان عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، عَنْ الْبَرَاءِ بْنِ عَازِبٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "مُؤْمِنُو أُمَّتِي شُهَدَاءُ". قَالَ: ثُمَّ تَلَا ﷺ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الصِّدِّيقُونَ وَالشُّهَدَاءُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ [لَهُمْ أَجْرُهُمْ] ﴾ هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ 

وَقَالَ أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مَيْمُونٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الصِّدِّيقُونَ وَالشُّهَدَاءُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ لَهُمْ أَجْرُهُمْ وَنُورُهُمْ﴾ قَالَ: يجيؤون يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ مَعًا كَالْإِصْبَعَيْنِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالشُّهَدَاءُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: فِي جَنَّاتِ النَّعِيمِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: "إِنَّ أَرْوَاحَ الشُّهَدَاءِ فِي حَوَاصِلِ طَيْرٍ خُضْر تَسْرَحُ فِي الْجَنَّةِ حَيْثُ شَاءَتْ، ثُمَّ تَأْوِي إِلَى تِلْكَ الْقَنَادِيلِ، فَاطَّلَعَ عَلَيْهِمْ رَبُّكَ اطِّلَاعَةً فَقَالَ: مَاذَا تُرِيدُونَ؟ فَقَالُوا: نُحِبُّ أَنْ تَرُدَّنَا إِلَى الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا فَنُقَاتِلَ فِيكَ فَنَقْتُلَ كَمَا قُتِلنا أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ. فَقَالَ إِنِّي قَضَيْتُ أَنَّهُمْ إِلَيْهَا لَا يَرْجِعُونَ" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَهُمْ أَجْرُهُمْ وَنُورُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَهُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ أَجْرٌ جَزِيلٌ وَنُورٌ عَظِيمٌ يَسْعَى بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ، وَهُمْ فِي ذَلِكَ يَتَفَاوَتُونَ بِحَسَبِ مَا كَانُوا فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا مِنَ الْأَعْمَالِ، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أحمد:

حدثنا يحيى ابن إسحاق، حدثنا بن لَهِيعَة، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ دِينَارٍ، عَنْ أَبِي يَزِيدَ الْخَوْلَانِيِّ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ فَضَالَةَ بْنَ عُبَيد يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ عُمَرَ بْنَ الْخَطَّابِ يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "الشُّهَدَاءُ أَرْبَعَةٌ: رَجُلٌ مُؤْمِنٌ جَيِّدُ الْإِيمَانِ، لَقِيَ الْعَدُوَّ فَصَدَقَ اللَّهَ فَقُتِلَ، فَذَلِكَ الَّذِي يَنْظُرُ النَّاسُ إِلَيْهِ هَكَذَا-وَرَفَعَ رَأْسَهُ حَتَّى سَقَطَتْ قَلَنْسُوة رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَوَ قَلَنْسُوَةُ عُمَرَ-وَالثَّانِي مُؤْمِنٌ لَقِيَ الْعَدُوَّ فَكَأَنَّمَا يَضْرِبُ ظَهْرَهُ بِشَوْكِ الطَّلْحِ، جَاءَهُ سَهْمٌ غَرْب فَقَتَلَهُ، فَذَاكَ فِي الدَّرَجَةِ الثَّانِيَةِ، وَالثَّالِثُ رَجُلٌ مُؤْمِنٌ خَلَطَ عَمَلًا صَالِحًا وَآخَرَ سَيِّئًا لَقِيَ الْعَدُوَّ فَصَدَقَ اللَّهَ حَتَّى قُتِلَ، فَذَاكَ فِي الدَّرَجَةِ الثَّالِثَةِ، وَالرَّابِعُ رَجُلٌ مُؤْمِنٌ أَسْرَفَ عَلَى نَفْسِهِ إِسْرَافًا كَثِيرًا، لَقِيَ الْعَدُوَّ فَصَدَقَ اللَّهَ حَتَّى قُتِلَ، فَذَاكَ فِي الدَّرَجَةِ الرَّابِعَةِ". 

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْمَدِينِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ الْمُبَارَكِ، عَنِ ابْنِ لَهِيعَة، وَقَالَ: هَذَا إِسْنَادٌ مِصْرِيٌّ صَالِحٌ. وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ لَهِيعَةَ وَقَالَ: حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَكَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا أُولَئِكَ أَصْحَابُ الْجَحِيمِ﴾ لَمَّا ذَكَرَ السُّعَدَاءَ وَمَآلَهُمْ، عَطَفَ بِذِكْرِ الأشقياء وبين حالهم.

---

## 57:20-21 — verses 20-21 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, diminishing the matter of worldly life and belittling it: {The life of this world is only play, diversion, adornment, mutual boasting among you, and rivalry in increase of wealth and children}. That is, the sum of its affair to its people is this, as He said: {Beautified for people is the love of desires, of women, children, heaped-up hoards of gold and silver, branded horses, cattle, and tilled land. That is the enjoyment of worldly life, but with God is the good return} [Al 'Imran: 14].

Then the Exalted struck a parable for worldly life, that it is a fading bloom and a vanishing blessing, and said: {Like a rain}, meaning the rain that comes after people have despaired, as He said: {And it is He who sends down the rain after they have despaired, and spreads His mercy} [al-Shura: 28].

His saying: {whose growth impresses the disbelievers}, meaning the growth of that crop which sprouted from the rain impresses the farmers. Just as that impresses the farmers, so too does worldly life impress the disbelievers, for they are the most eager of all creatures for it and the most inclined of people toward it. {Then it withers and you see it turn yellow, then it becomes broken debris}, meaning that crop withers and you see it turn yellow after having been green and fresh, then after all that it becomes broken debris, that is, it becomes dry and crumbled. Such is worldly life: it is first young, then it reaches middle age, then it becomes an old and unsightly woman. Likewise a human being, in the first part of his life and the prime of his youth, is fresh, tender, supple of limb, and pleasant to look at. Then he begins to enter middle age, his nature changes, and some of his strength is spent. Then he grows old and becomes an elderly man, weak in strength, little in movement, overcome by the slightest thing, as the Exalted said: {God is the One who created you from weakness, then made after weakness strength, then made after strength weakness and gray hair. He creates what He wills, and He is the All-Knowing, the All-Capable} [al-Rum: 54].

Since this parable indicates the passing away of this world, its termination, and its inevitable emptying out, and that the Hereafter is coming without doubt, He warned against its matter and encouraged what good lies within it, and said: {And in the Hereafter is severe punishment, and forgiveness from God and approval. And the life of this world is nothing but the enjoyment of delusion}, meaning that in the coming, near Hereafter there is nothing but one of two things: either severe punishment, or forgiveness from God and approval.

His saying: {And the life of this world is nothing but the enjoyment of delusion}, meaning it is a fleeting, deceptive enjoyment for whoever relies upon it, for he is deceived by it and it delights him until he believes there is no abode besides it and no return beyond it, while it is trifling and small in comparison to the abode of the Hereafter.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "A place the size of a whip in Paradise is better than this world and all that is in it. Recite: {And the life of this world is nothing but the enjoyment of delusion}."

This hadith is established in the Sahih without this addition. And God knows best.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abdullah said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Paradise is nearer to any one of you than the strap of his sandal, and likewise the Fire."

Al-Bukhari alone recorded it, in "al-Riqaq," from the hadith of al-Thawri, from al-A'mash, with this chain.

In this hadith is evidence of the nearness of good and evil to a human being. Since the matter is so, God urged him to hasten toward good deeds, performing acts of obedience and abandoning what is forbidden, things which expiate sins and lapses for him and secure for him reward and elevated ranks. The Exalted said: {Race toward forgiveness from your Lord and a garden whose width is like the width of heaven and earth}. What is meant is the type of heaven and earth, as He said in another verse: {And hasten to forgiveness from your Lord and a garden whose width is the heavens and the earth, prepared for the righteous} [Al 'Imran: 133]. And here He said: {prepared for those who believe in God and His messengers. That is the bounty of God which He gives to whom He wills, and God is the Possessor of great bounty}, meaning that this which God has qualified them for is from His bounty, His favor upon them, and His kindness to them.

As we mentioned previously in the Sahih: that the poor among the Emigrants said, "O Messenger of God, the wealthy have taken away the highest ranks and the everlasting bliss." He said, "How is that?" They said, "They pray as we pray, they fast as we fast, but they give charity while we cannot give charity, and they free slaves while we cannot free slaves." He said, "Shall I not tell you of something by which, if you do it, you will overtake those before you and none will be better than you except one who does the same as you: you glorify God, magnify Him, and praise Him thirty-three times after every prayer." He said: They returned and said, "Our brothers, the wealthy, heard what we did and did the same!" So the Messenger of God ﷺ said, "That is the bounty of God which He gives to whom He wills."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُوهنًا أَمْرَ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَمُحَقِّرًا لَهَا: ﴿أَنَّمَا الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا لَعِبٌ وَلَهْوٌ وَزِينَةٌ وَتَفَاخُرٌ بَيْنَكُمْ وَتَكَاثُرٌ فِي الأمْوَالِ وَالأوْلادِ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا حَاصِلُ أَمْرِهَا عِنْدَ أَهْلِهَا هَذَا، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿زُيِّنَ لِلنَّاسِ حُبُّ الشَّهَوَاتِ مِنَ النِّسَاءِ وَالْبَنِينَ وَالْقَنَاطِيرِ الْمُقَنْطَرَةِ مِنَ الذَّهَبِ وَالْفِضَّةِ وَالْخَيْلِ الْمُسَوَّمَةِ وَالأنْعَامِ وَالْحَرْثِ ذَلِكَ مَتَاعُ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَاللَّهُ عِنْدَهُ حُسْنُ الْمَآبِ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٤]

ثُمَّ ضَرَبَ تَعَالَى مَثَلَ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا فِي أَنَّهَا زَهْرَةٌ فَانِيَةٌ وَنِعْمَةٌ زَائِلَةٌ فَقَالَ: ﴿كَمَثَلِ غَيْثٍ﴾ وَهُوَ: الْمَطَرُ الَّذِي يَأْتِي بَعْدَ قُنُوطِ النَّاسِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي يُنزلُ الْغَيْثَ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا قَنَطُوا [وَيَنْشُرُ رَحْمَتَهُ] ﴾ [الشُّورَى: ٢٨] 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَعْجَبَ الْكُفَّارَ نَبَاتُهُ﴾ أَيْ: يُعْجِبُ الزُّرَّاعَ نَبَاتُ ذَلِكَ الزَّرْعِ الَّذِي نَبَتَ بِالْغَيْثِ؛ وَكَمَا يُعْجِبُ الزُّرَّاعَ ذَلِكَ كَذَلِكَ تُعْجِبُ الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا الْكُفَّارَ، فَإِنَّهُمْ أَحْرَصُ شَيْءٍ عَلَيْهَا وَأَمْيَلُ النَّاسِ إِلَيْهَا، ﴿ثُمَّ يَهِيجُ فَتَرَاهُ مُصْفَرًّا ثُمَّ يَكُونُ حُطَامًا﴾ أَيْ: يَهِيجُ ذَلِكَ الزَّرْعُ فَتَرَاهُ مُصْفَرًّا بَعْدَ مَا كَانَ خَضِرًا نَضِرًا، ثُمَّ يَكُونُ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ كُلُّهُ حُطَامًا، أَيْ: يَصِيرُ يَبَسًا مُتَحَطِّمًا، هَكَذَا الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا تَكُونُ أَوَّلًا شَابَّةً، ثُمَّ تَكْتَهِلُ، ثُمَّ تَكُونُ عَجُوزًا شَوْهَاءَ، وَالْإِنْسَانُ كَذَلِكَ فِي أَوَّلِ عُمْرِهِ وَعُنْفُوَانِ شَبَابِهِ غَضًّا طَرِيًّا لَيِّنَ الْأَعْطَافِ، بَهِيَّ الْمَنْظَرِ، ثُمَّ إِنَّهُ يَشْرَعُ فِي الْكُهُولَةِ فَتَتَغَيَّرُ طِبَاعُهُ وَيَنْفَد بَعْضُ قُوَاهُ، ثُمَّ يَكْبَرُ فَيَصِيرُ شَيْخًا كَبِيرًا، ضَعِيفَ الْقُوَى، قَلِيلَ الْحَرَكَةِ، يُعْجِزُهُ الشَّيْءُ الْيَسِيرُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿اللَّهُ الَّذِي خَلَقَكُمْ مِنْ ضَعْفٍ ثُمَّ جَعَلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ ضَعْفٍ قُوَّةً ثُمَّ جَعَلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ قُوَّةٍ ضَعْفًا وَشَيْبَةً يَخْلُقُ مَا يَشَاءُ وَهُوَ الْعَلِيمُ الْقَدِيرُ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٥٤] . وَلَمَّا كَانَ هَذَا الْمَثَلُ دَالًّا عَلَى زَوَالِ الدُّنْيَا وَانْقِضَائِهَا وَفَرَاغِهَا لَا مَحَالَةَ، وَأَنَّ الْآخِرَةَ كَائِنَةٌ لَا مَحَالَةَ، حَذّر مِنْ أَمْرِهَا وَرَغَّبَ فِيمَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْخَيْرِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَفِي الآخِرَةِ عَذَابٌ شَدِيدٌ وَمَغْفِرَةٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَرِضْوَانٌ وَمَا الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا إِلا مَتَاعُ الْغُرُورِ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَيْسَ فِي الْآخِرَةِ الْآتِيَةِ الْقَرِيبَةِ إِلَّا إِمَّا هَذَا وَإِمَّا هَذَا: إِمَّا عَذَابٌ شَدِيدٌ، وَإِمَّا مَغْفِرَةٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَرِضْوَانٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا إِلا مَتَاعُ الْغُرُورِ﴾ أَيْ: هِيَ مَتَاعٌ فانٍ غارٍّ لمن ركن إليه فإنه يغتر بِهَا وَتُعْجِبُهُ حَتَّى يَعْتَقِدَ أَنَّهُ لَا دَارَ سِوَاهَا وَلَا مَعَادَ وَرَاءَهَا، وَهِيَ حَقِيرَةٌ قَلِيلَةٌ بِالنِّسْبَةِ إِلَى الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلَيُّ ابْنُ حَرْبٍ الْمَوْصِلِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا الْمُحَارِبِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَوْضِعُ سَوْطٍ فِي الجنة خير من الدنيا وما فيها. اقرؤوا: ﴿وَمَا الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا إِلا مَتَاعُ الْغُرُورِ﴾ 

وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ ثَابِتٌ فِي الصَّحِيحِ بِدُونِ هَذِهِ الزِّيَادَةِ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ نُمَيْرٍ ووَكِيع، كِلَاهُمَا عَنِ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ شَقِيقٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَلْجنة أَقْرَبُ إِلَى أَحَدِكُمْ مِنْ شِرَاك نَعْلِهِ، وَالنَّارُ مِثْلُ ذَلِكَ".

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ فِي "الرِّقَاقِ"، مِنْ حَدِيثِ الثَّوْرِيِّ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، بِهِ 

فَفِي هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ دَلِيلٌ عَلَى اقْتِرَابِ الْخَيْرِ وَالشَّرِّ مِنَ الْإِنْسَانِ، وَإِذَا كَانَ الْأَمْرُ كَذَلِكَ؛ فَلِهَذَا حَثَّهُ اللَّهُ عَلَى الْمُبَادَرَةِ إِلَى الْخَيْرَاتِ، مِنْ فِعْلِ الطَّاعَاتِ، وَتَرْكِ الْمُحَرَّمَاتِ، الَّتِي تُكَفِّرُ عَنْهُ الذُّنُوبَ وَالزَّلَّاتِ، وَتُحَصِّلُ لَهُ الثَّوَابَ وَالدَّرَجَاتِ، فَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿سَابِقُوا إِلَى مَغْفِرَةٍ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ وَجَنَّةٍ عَرْضُهَا كَعَرْضِ السَّمَاءِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ وَالْمُرَادُ جِنْسُ السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَسَارِعُوا إِلَى مَغْفِرَةٍ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ وَجَنَّةٍ عَرْضُهَا السَّمَاوَاتُ وَالأرْضُ أُعِدَّتْ لِلْمُتَّقِينَ﴾ [آل عمران: ١٣٣] . وقال هاهنا: ﴿أُعِدَّتْ لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ ذَلِكَ فَضْلُ اللَّهِ يُؤْتِيهِ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَاللَّهُ ذُو الْفَضْلِ الْعَظِيمِ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا الَّذِي أَهَّلَهُمُ اللَّهُ لَهُ هُوَ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ وَمَنِّهِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَإِحْسَانِهِ إِلَيْهِمْ، كَمَا قدَّمنا فِي الصَّحِيحِ: أَنَّ فُقَرَاءَ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ قَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، ذَهَبَ أَهْلُ الدُّثور بِالدَّرَجَاتِ الْعُلَى وَالنَّعِيمِ الْمُقِيمِ. قَالَ: "وَمَا ذَاكَ؟ ". قَالُوا: يُصلُّون كَمَا نُصَلِّي، وَيَصُومُونَ كَمَا نَصُومُ، وَيَتَصَدَّقُونَ وَلَا نَتَصَدَّقُ، ويُعتقون وَلَا نُعْتِق. قَالَ: "أَفَلَا أَدُلُّكُمْ عَلَى شَيْءٍ إِذَا فَعَلْتُمُوهُ سَبَقْتُمْ مَنْ بَعْدَكُمْ، وَلَا يَكُونُ أَحَدٌ أَفْضَلَ مِنْكُمْ إِلَّا مَنْ صَنَعَ مِثْلَ مَا صَنَعْتُمْ: تُسَبِّحُونَ وَتُكَبِّرُونَ وَتَحْمَدُونَ دُبُر كُلِّ صَلَاةٍ ثَلَاثًا وَثَلَاثِينَ". قَالَ: فَرَجَعُوا فَقَالُوا: سَمِعَ إِخْوَانُنَا أَهْلُ الْأَمْوَالِ مَا فَعَلْنَا، فَفَعَلُوا مِثْلَهُ! فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "ذَلِكَ فَضْلُ اللَّهِ يؤتيه من يشاء"

---

## 57:22-24 — verses 22-24 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs about His decree that preceded His creation, before He created the created beings, saying: {No misfortune strikes upon the earth or in yourselves} meaning: in the horizons and in yourselves, {except that it is in a record before We bring it into being} meaning: before We created the creation and brought forth the souls.

Some of them said: {before We bring it into being} refers back to the souls. It was also said that it refers back to the misfortune. But the best view is that it refers back to the creation and the created beings, since the wording indicates this, as Ibn Jarir said:

[chain] Ya'qub told me, Ibn Ulayyah told us, from Mansur ibn Abd al-Rahman, who said: I was sitting with al-Hasan when a man said, "Ask him about His saying: {No misfortune strikes upon the earth or in yourselves except that it is in a record before We bring it into being}." So I asked him about it, and he said: "Glory be to God! Who would doubt this? Every misfortune between heaven and earth is in the Book of God before the souls were created."

Qatada said regarding {No misfortune strikes upon the earth}: this refers to the years, meaning drought, and regarding {or in yourselves}: he said, this refers to pains and illnesses. He said: it has reached us that no one is afflicted by the scratch of a stick, nor the stumbling of a foot, nor the twitching of a vein, except on account of a sin, and what God pardons is far greater.

This noble verse is among the clearest proofs against the Qadariyyah who deny the prior knowledge of God, may God disfigure them. Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Abu Abd al-Rahman told us, Haywah and Ibn Lahi'ah told us, they said Abu Hani' al-Khawlani told us: that he heard Abu Abd al-Rahman al-Hubuli say: I heard Abdullah ibn Amr ibn al-As say: I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "God decreed the measures of all things fifty thousand years before He created the heavens and the earth."

Muslim related it in his Sahih, from the hadith of Abdullah ibn Wahb, Haywah ibn Shurayh, and Nafi' ibn Yazid, all three of them from Abu Hani', with the same wording. Ibn Wahb added: "and His Throne was upon the water." Al-Tirmidhi also related it and said: hasan sahih (a sound, authentic report).

His saying {Indeed that is easy for God} means: that His, the Exalted's, knowledge of things before they exist, and His recording of them exactly as they will occur in their time, is easy for God, mighty and glorious, because He knows what has been, what will be, and what would have been had it been, and how it would have occurred.

His saying {so that you may not grieve over what has passed you by, nor rejoice in what has come to you} means: We have informed you of the precedence of Our knowledge and the priority of Our recording of things before they come into being, and Our decreeing of created things before their existence, so that you may know that what befell you was not going to miss you, and what missed you was not going to befall you. So do not grieve over what has passed you by, for indeed if a thing was decreed, it would occur. {Nor rejoice in what has come to you} meaning: what has reached you. It is also read as "ataakum," meaning: what He has given you. Both readings are interconnected in meaning, that is: do not boast before people over what God has bestowed upon you as a favor, for that is not by your own effort or exertion, but rather it is by God's decree and His provision for you. So do not take God's favors as an occasion for insolence and arrogance, boasting with them over people. Hence He said: {And God does not love every arrogant boaster} meaning: one who is self-conceited, arrogant, and boastful, that is, over others.

Ikrimah said: there is no one but that he rejoices and grieves, but make your joy an occasion for gratitude and your grief an occasion for patience.

Then He said: {Those who are miserly and enjoin miserliness upon people} meaning: they do what is forbidden and incite people toward it. {And whoever turns away} meaning: from God's command and obedience to Him, {then indeed God is the Self-Sufficient, the Praiseworthy}, just as Moses (peace be upon him) said: {If you disbelieve, you and all who are on the earth, then indeed God is Self-Sufficient, Praiseworthy} [Ibrahim: 8].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ قَدَرِهِ السَّابِقِ فِي خَلْقِهِ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَبْرَأَ الْبَرِيَّةَ فَقَالَ: ﴿مَا أَصَابَ مِنْ مُصِيبَةٍ فِي الأرْضِ وَلا فِي أَنْفُسِكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الْآفَاقِ وَفِي نُفُوسِكُمْ ﴿إِلا فِي كِتَابٍ مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ نَبْرَأَهَا﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ نَخْلُقَ الْخَلِيقَةَ وَنَبْرَأَ النَّسَمَةَ.

وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: ﴿مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ نَبْرَأَهَا﴾ عَائِدٌ عَلَى النُّفُوسِ. وَقِيلَ: عَائِدٌ عَلَى الْمُصِيبَةِ. وَالْأَحْسَنُ عَوْدُهُ عَلَى الْخَلِيقَةِ وَالْبَرِيَّةِ؛ لِدَلَالَةِ الْكَلَامِ عَلَيْهَا، كَمَا قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ:

حَدَّثَنِي يَعْقُوبُ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عُلَيَّة، عَنْ مَنْصُورِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ قَالَ: كُنْتُ جَالِسًا مَعَ الْحَسَنِ، فَقَالَ رَجُلٌ: سَلْهُ عَنْ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿مَا أَصَابَ مِنْ مُصِيبَةٍ فِي الأرْضِ وَلا فِي أَنْفُسِكُمْ إِلا فِي كِتَابٍ مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ نَبْرَأَهَا﴾ فَسَأَلْتُهُ عَنْهَا، فَقَالَ: سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ! وَمَنْ يَشُكُّ فِي هَذَا؟ كُلُّ مُصِيبَةٍ بَيْنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ، فَفِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ يَبْرَأَ النَّسَمَةَ 

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿مَا أَصَابَ مِنْ مُصِيبَةٍ فِي الأرْضِ﴾ قَالَ: هِيَ السُّنُونَ. يَعْنِي: الجَدْب، ﴿وَلا فِي أَنْفُسِكُمْ﴾ يَقُولُ: الْأَوْجَاعُ وَالْأَمْرَاضُ. قَالَ: وَبَلَغَنَا أَنَّهُ لَيْسَ أَحَدٌ يُصِيبُهُ خَدْشُ عُودٍ وَلَا نَكْبَةُ قَدَمٍ، وَلَا خَلَجَانُ عَرَقٍ إِلَّا بِذَنْبٍ، وَمَا يَعْفُو اللَّهُ عَنْهُ أَكْثَرُ.

وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ الْكَرِيمَةُ مِنْ أَدَلِّ دَلِيلٍ عَلَى القَدَرية نُفاة الْعِلْمِ السَّابِقِ-قَبَّحَهُمُ اللَّهُ-وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، حَدَّثَنَا حَيْوَةُ وَابْنُ لَهِيعة قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو هَانِئٍ الْخَوْلَانِيُّ: أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ أَبَا عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الحُبُلي يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمرو بْنِ الْعَاصِ يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "قدَّر الله المقادير قَبْلَ أَنْ يَخْلُقَ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ بِخَمْسِينَ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ".

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ وَهْبٍ وَحَيْوَةَ بْنِ شُرَيْحٍ وَنَافِعِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ، وَثَلَاثَتُهُمْ عَنْ أَبِي هَانِئٍ، بِهِ. وَزَادَ بْنُ وَهب: "وَكَانَ عَرْشُهُ عَلَى الْمَاءِ". وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَقَالَ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ ذَلِكَ عَلَى اللَّهِ يَسِيرٌ﴾ أَيْ: أَنَّ عِلْمَهُ تَعَالَى الْأَشْيَاءَ قَبْلَ كَوْنِهَا وَكِتَابَتَهُ لَهَا طِبْقَ مَا يُوجَدُ فِي حِينِهَا سَهْلٌ عَلَى اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ ؛ لِأَنَّهُ يَعْلَمُ مَا كَانَ وَمَا يَكُونُ وَمَا لَمْ يَكُنْ لَوْ كَانَ كيف كان يكون.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِكَيْ لَا تَأْسَوْا عَلَى مَا فَاتَكُمْ وَلا تَفْرَحُوا بِمَا آتَاكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَعْلَمْنَاكُمْ بِتَقَدُّمِ عِلْمِنَا وَسَبْقِ كِتَابَتِنَا لِلْأَشْيَاءِ قَبْلَ كَوْنِهَا، وَتَقْدِيرِنَا الْكَائِنَاتِ قَبْلَ وُجُودِهَا، لِتَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ مَا أَصَابَكُمْ لَمْ يَكُنْ لِيُخْطِئَكُمْ، وَمَا أَخْطَأَكُمْ لَمْ يَكُنْ لِيُصِيبَكُمْ، فَلَا تَأْسَوْا عَلَى مَا فَاتَكُمْ، فَإِنَّهُ لَوْ قُدِّرَ شَيْءٌ لَكَانَ ﴿وَلا تَفْرَحُوا بِمَا آتَاكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: جَاءَكُمْ، وَيَقْرَأُ: "آتاكُم" أَيْ: أَعْطَاكُمْ. وَكِلَاهُمَا مُتَلَازِمَانِ، أَيْ: لَا تَفْخَرُوا عَلَى النَّاسِ بِمَا أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ بِهِ عَلَيْكُمْ، فَإِنَّ ذَلِكَ لَيْسَ بِسَعْيِكُمْ وَلَا كَدِّكُمْ، وَإِنَّمَا هُوَ عَنْ قَدَرِ اللَّهِ وَرِزْقِهِ لَكُمْ، فَلَا تَتَّخِذُوا نِعَمَ اللَّهِ أَشَرًا وَبَطَرًا، تَفْخَرُونَ بِهَا عَلَى النَّاسِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَاللَّهُ لَا يُحِبُّ كُلَّ مُخْتَالٍ فَخُورٍ﴾ أَيْ: مُخْتَالٍ فِي نَفْسِهِ مُتَكَبِّرٍ فَخُورٍ، أَيْ: عَلَى غَيْرِهِ.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: لَيْسَ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا وَهُوَ يَفْرَحُ وَيَحْزَنُ، وَلَكِنِ اجْعَلُوا الفَرَح شُكْرًا وَالْحُزْنَ صَبْرًا.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿الَّذِينَ يَبْخَلُونَ وَيَأْمُرُونَ النَّاسَ بِالْبُخْلِ﴾ أَيْ: يَفْعَلُونَ الْمُنْكَرَ وَيَحُضُّونَ النَّاسَ عَلَيْهِ، ﴿وَمَنْ يَتَوَلَّ﴾ أَيْ: عَنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ وَطَاعَتِهِ ﴿فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ الْغَنِيُّ الْحَمِيدُ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ مُوسَى عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: ﴿إِنْ تَكْفُرُوا أَنْتُمْ وَمَنْ فِي الأرْضِ جَمِيعًا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَغَنِيٌّ حَمِيدٌ﴾ [إبراهيم: ٨] .

---

## 57:25 — verse 25

### Translation

The Almighty says: {We have indeed sent Our messengers with clear proofs} that is, with miracles, decisive arguments, and conclusive evidences, {and We sent down with them the Book} which is the transmitted report that confirms, {and the Balance} which is justice. This is what Mujahid, Qatadah, and others said. It is the truth to which sound, upright minds bear witness, minds that oppose corrupt opinions, as He said: {Is he who has a clear proof from his Lord, followed by a witness from Him...} [Hud: 17], and He said: {The nature which Allah instilled in mankind} [al-Rum: 30], and He said: {And the heaven He raised, and He set up the Balance} [al-Rahman: 7]. This is why He says in this verse: {so that mankind may establish justice}, that is, truth and fairness, which consists of following the messengers in what they reported and obeying them in what they commanded. For what they brought is the truth beyond which there is no further truth, as He said: {And the word of your Lord has been completed in truth and justice} [al-An'am: 115], meaning: truthful in its reports, and just in its commands and prohibitions. This is why the believers say, when they settle into the chambers of the gardens, the lofty dwellings, and the arrayed couches: {Praise be to Allah who has guided us to this. We would never have been guided if Allah had not guided us. The messengers of our Lord have indeed come with the truth} [al-A'raf: 43].

His statement: {And We sent down iron, in which is great might} means: We made iron a deterrent for whoever refuses the truth and stubbornly opposes it after the argument has been established against him. This is why the Messenger of Allah ﷺ remained in Mecca for thirteen years after prophethood, receiving the Meccan surahs by revelation, all of which consist of argumentation with the polytheists, clarification and elucidation of the oneness of Allah (tawhid), explanation, and proofs. When the argument had been firmly established against those who opposed it, Allah prescribed migration (hijrah) and commanded them to fight with swords, striking the necks and heads of whoever opposed the Qur'an, denied it, and stubbornly resisted it.

Imam Ahmad and Abu Dawud narrated, from the hadith of Abd al-Rahman ibn Thabit ibn Thawban, from Hassan ibn Atiyyah, from Abu al-Munib al-Jurashi al-Shami, from Ibn Umar, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I have been sent with the sword just before the Hour, until Allah alone is worshipped with no partner. My provision has been placed under the shadow of my spear, and abasement and humiliation have been placed upon whoever opposes my command. Whoever imitates a people becomes one of them."

This is why the Almighty said: {in which is great might}, meaning weapons such as swords, spears, spearheads, arrowheads, armor, and the like. {And benefits for mankind}, meaning in their livelihoods, such as the plow-blade, the axe, the adze, the saw, the chisel, the shovel, and the tools that assist in farming, weaving, cooking, baking, and other things without which people cannot sustain their affairs.

Ilba' ibn Ahmad reported, from Ikrimah, that Ibn Abbas said: Three things came down with Adam: the anvil, the tongs, and the miqa'ah, meaning the hammer. Narrated by Ibn Jarir and Ibn Abi Hatim.

His statement: {and that Allah may know who supports Him and His messengers, unseen} means: whoever's intention in carrying weapons is to support Allah and His messengers. {Indeed Allah is Strong, Mighty} that is, He is Strong and Mighty, He supports whoever supports Him, without any need on His part for people. Rather, He prescribed jihad in order to test some of you by means of others.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَقَدْ أَرْسَلْنَا رُسُلَنَا بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْمُعْجِزَاتِ، وَالْحُجَجِ الْبَاهِرَاتِ، وَالدَّلَائِلِ الْقَاطِعَاتِ، ﴿وَأَنزلْنَا مَعَهُمُ الْكِتَابَ﴾ وَهُوَ: النَّقْلُ الْمُصَدِّقُ ﴿وَالْمِيزَانَ﴾ وَهُوَ: الْعَدْلُ. قَالَهُ مُجَاهِدٌ، وقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُهُمَا. وَهُوَ الْحَقُّ الَّذِي تَشْهَدُ بِهِ الْعُقُولُ الصَّحِيحَةُ الْمُسْتَقِيمَةُ الْمُخَالِفَةُ لِلْآرَاءِ السَّقِيمَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿أَفَمَنْ كَانَ عَلَى بَيِّنَةٍ مِنْ رَبِّهِ وَيَتْلُوهُ شَاهِدٌ مِنْهُ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٧] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿فِطْرَةَ اللَّهِ الَّتِي فَطَرَ النَّاسَ عَلَيْهَا﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٣٠] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَالسَّمَاءَ رَفَعَهَا وَوَضَعَ الْمِيزَانَ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ: ٧] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿لِيَقُومَ النَّاسُ بِالْقِسْطِ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْحَقِّ وَالْعَدْلِ وَهُوَ: اتِّبَاعُ الرُّسُلِ فِيمَا أَخْبَرُوا بِهِ، وَطَاعَتُهُمْ فِيمَا أَمَرُوا بِهِ، فَإِنَّ الذي جاؤوا بِهِ هُوَ الْحَقُّ الَّذِي لَيْسَ وَرَاءَهُ حَقٌّ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَتَمَّتْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ صِدْقًا وَعَدْلا﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١١٥] أَيْ: صِدْقًا فِي الْأَخْبَارِ، وَعَدْلًا فِي الْأَوَامِرِ وَالنَّوَاهِي. ولهذا يقول المؤمنون إذا تبوؤوا غُرَفَ الْجَنَّاتِ، وَالْمَنَازِلَ الْعَالِيَاتِ، وَالسُّرُرَ الْمَصْفُوفَاتِ: ﴿الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي هَدَانَا لِهَذَا وَمَا كُنَّا لِنَهْتَدِيَ لَوْلا أَنْ هَدَانَا اللَّهُ لَقَدْ جَاءَتْ رُسُلُ رَبِّنَا بِالْحَقِّ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٤٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَنزلْنَا الْحَدِيدَ فِيهِ بَأْسٌ شَدِيدٌ﴾ أَيْ: وَجَعَلْنَا الْحَدِيدَ رَادِعًا لِمَنْ أَبَى الْحَقَّ وَعَانَدَهُ بَعْدَ قِيَامِ الْحُجَّةِ عَلَيْهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا أَقَامَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِمَكَّةَ بَعْدَ النُّبُوَّةِ ثَلَاثَ عَشْرَةَ سَنَةً تُوحَى إِلَيْهِ السُّوَرُ الْمَكِّيَّةُ، وَكُلُّهَا جِدَالٌ مَعَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، وَبَيَانٌ وَإِيضَاحٌ لِلتَّوْحِيدِ، وَتِبْيَانٌ وَدَلَائِلُ، فَلَمَّا قَامَتِ الْحُجَّةُ عَلَى مَنْ خَالَفَ شَرَعَ اللَّهُ الْهِجْرَةَ، وَأَمَرَهُمْ بِالْقِتَالِ بِالسُّيُوفِ، وَضَرْبِ الرِّقَابِ وَالْهَامِ لِمَنْ خَالَفَ الْقُرْآنَ وَكَذَّبَ بِهِ وَعَانَدَهُ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ ثَابِتِ بْنِ ثَوْبَانَ، عَنْ حَسَّانَ بْنِ عَطِيَّةَ، عَنْ أَبِي الْمُنِيبِ الْجُرَشِيِّ الشَّامِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "بُعِثتُ بِالسَّيْفِ بَيْنَ يَدَي السَّاعَةِ حَتَّى يُعبَد اللَّهُ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وجُعِل رِزْقِي تَحْتَ ظِلّ رُمْحي، وَجَعَلَ الذِّلَّةُ والصِّغار عَلَى مَنْ خَالَفَ أَمْرِي، وَمَنْ تَشبَّه بِقَوْمٍ فَهُوَ مِنْهُمْ" 

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فِيهِ بَأْسٌ شَدِيدٌ﴾ يَعْنِي: السِّلَاحَ كَالسُّيُوفِ، وَالْحِرَابِ، وَالسِّنَانِ، وَالنِّصَالَ، وَالدُّرُوعِ، وَنَحْوِهَا. ﴿وَمَنَافِعُ لِلنَّاسِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي مَعَايِشِهِمْ كَالسِّكَّةِ وَالْفَأْسِ وَالْقَدُومِ، وَالْمِنْشَارِ، وَالْإِزْمِيلِ، وَالْمِجْرَفَةِ، وَالْآلَاتِ الَّتِي يُسْتَعَانُ بِهَا فِي الْحِرَاثَةِ وَالْحِيَاكَةِ وَالطَّبْخِ وَالْخَبْزِ وَمَا لَا قِوَامَ لِلنَّاسِ بِدُونِهِ، وَغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ.

قَالَ عِلْباء بْنُ أَحْمَدَ، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، أَنَّ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: ثَلَاثَةُ أَشْيَاءَ نَزَلَتْ مَعَ آدَمَ: السَّنْدَانُ والكلْبَتان والميقعَة -يَعْنِي الْمِطْرَقَةَ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلِيَعْلَمَ اللَّهُ مَنْ يَنْصُرُهُ وَرُسُلَهُ بِالْغَيْبِ﴾ أَيْ: مَنْ نِيَّتُهُ فِي حَمْلِ السِّلَاحِ نُصْرَةُ اللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ، ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَوِيٌّ عَزِيزٌ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ قَوِيٌّ عَزِيزٌ، يَنْصُرُ مَنْ نَصَرَهُ مِنْ غَيْرِ احْتِيَاجٍ مِنْهُ إِلَى النَّاسِ، وَإِنَّمَا شَرَعَ الْجِهَادَ لِيَبْلُوَ بَعْضَكُمْ بِبَعْضٍ.

---

## 57:26-27 — verses 26-27 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs that since He sent Nuh (peace be upon him), He did not send after him any messenger or prophet except from his progeny. Likewise Ibrahim (peace be upon him), the intimate friend of the Merciful, no scripture was sent down from heaven, no messenger was sent, and no revelation was given to any human being after him, except that he was from his lineage, as He said in another verse: {And We placed in the progeny of both of them prophethood and scripture}, until the last of the prophets of the Children of Israel was Isa son of Maryam, who gave glad tidings of Muhammad ﷺ after him, may the prayers and peace of Allah be upon both of them. For this reason the Almighty said: {Then We caused Our messengers to follow in their footsteps, and We caused Isa son of Maryam to follow, and We gave him the Gospel}.

This is the scripture which Allah revealed to him. {And We placed in the hearts of those who followed him}, meaning the disciples (hawariyyun), {compassion and mercy}, that is, compassion which is awe (khashyah), {and mercy} toward His creation.

His saying, {and monasticism which they invented}, means the community of the Christians invented it, {We did not prescribe it for them}, that is, We did not legislate it for them; rather they took it upon themselves of their own accord.

Regarding His saying, {except seeking the pleasure of Allah}, there are two opinions. One is that they intended by that the pleasure of Allah, as said by Sa'id ibn Jubayr and Qatadah. The other is: We did not prescribe that for them; rather We prescribed for them the seeking of Allah's pleasure.

His saying, {but they did not observe it as it should rightly be observed}, means they did not fulfill what they had taken upon themselves as it ought rightly to be fulfilled. This is a censure of them from two angles. The first is regarding the innovation in the religion of Allah of something Allah had not commanded. The second is regarding their failure to fulfill what they had taken upon themselves of that which they claimed was a means of nearness bringing them close to Allah, Mighty and Majestic.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Mas'ud said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to me, "O Ibn Mas'ud." I said, "At your service, O Messenger of Allah." He said, "Do you know that the Children of Israel split into seventy-two sects, none of which was saved except three sects, which stood up among the kings and tyrants after Isa son of Maryam (peace be upon him), calling to the religion of Allah and the religion of Isa son of Maryam. They fought the tyrants and were killed, but they were patient and were saved. Then another group arose who did not have the strength to fight, so they stood up among the kings and tyrants and called to the religion of Allah and the religion of Isa son of Maryam. They were killed, sawn apart with saws, and burned with fire, but they were patient and were saved. Then another group arose who did not have the strength to fight and could not bear to uphold justice, so they retreated to the mountains, worshipping and adopting monasticism. They are the ones whom Allah, Mighty and Majestic, mentioned: {and monasticism which they invented, We did not prescribe it for them}."

Ibn Jarir narrated it with different wording through another chain, saying: [chain] Abdullah ibn Mas'ud said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Those before us split into seventy-three sects, of which three were saved and the rest perished..." and he mentioned something similar to what preceded, and in it: "{So We gave those among them who believed their reward}, they are those who believed in me and confirmed me, {but many of them are transgressors}, they are those who denied me and opposed me."

This corroborating narration is not undermined by the condition of Dawud ibn al-Muhabbar, for he is one of the fabricators of hadith, but Abu Ya'la related it with an isnad, and his chain goes through Shayban ibn Farrukh, from al-Sa'q ibn Hazn, with the same content, so the hadith is strengthened from this route.

Ibn Jarir and Abu Abd al-Rahman al-Nasa'i said, and the wording is his: [chain] Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with both of them, said: There were kings after Isa (peace be upon him) who altered the Torah and the Gospel. Among them were believers who read the Torah and the Gospel, and it was said to their kings: "We find nothing more severe than the abuse these people hurl at us. They recite: {And whoever does not judge by what Allah has revealed, those are the disbelievers} [al-Ma'idah: 44], these verses, along with what they fault us for in our deeds when they recite. So summon them to recite as we recite and believe as we believe." So he summoned them, gathered them, and offered them either death or abandoning the recitation of the Torah and the Gospel except for what had been altered from it. They said, "What do you want from that? Leave us be." A group of them said, "Build us a pillar, then raise us up to it, then give us something with which to hoist our food and drink, and we will not return to you." Another group said, "Let us wander the earth roaming freely, drinking as wild beasts drink; if you can catch us in your land, then kill us." Another group said, "Build us houses in the wilderness, and we will dig wells and cultivate herbs, and we will not return to you nor pass by you." There was no one among the tribes but had a close relative among them, so they did this. Then Allah, Mighty and Majestic, revealed: {and monasticism which they invented, We did not prescribe it for them except seeking the pleasure of Allah, but they did not observe it as it should rightly be observed}. The others said, "We shall worship as so-and-so worshipped, wander as so-and-so wandered, and take houses as so-and-so took houses," while they remained upon their idolatry, having no knowledge of the faith of those they imitated. Then when the Prophet ﷺ was sent, and only a few of them remained, a man descended from his hermitage, a wanderer came from his wandering, and the master of the monastery came from his monastery, and they believed in him and confirmed him. So Allah, Mighty and Majestic, said: {O you who believe, fear Allah and believe in His Messenger; He will give you a double portion of His mercy}, two rewards for their belief in Isa son of Maryam, the Torah and the Gospel, and for their belief in Muhammad ﷺ and their confirmation of him. He said: {and make for you a light by which you will walk} [al-Hadid: 28], meaning the Qur'an, and their following of the Prophet ﷺ. He said: {so that the People of the Book may know}, those who resemble you, {that they have no power over anything of the bounty of Allah, and that all bounty is in the hand of Allah; He gives it to whom He wills, and Allah is possessor of great bounty}.

This account contains gharabah (an unusual or singular quality), and the interpretation of these other two verses will come later differently from this, and Allah knows best.

The hafiz Abu Ya'la al-Mawsili said: [chain] Sahl ibn Abi Umamah related that he and his father entered upon Anas ibn Malik in Madinah during the time of Umar ibn Abd al-Aziz, while he was governor, and Anas was praying a light prayer, as if it were the prayer of a traveler or close to it. When he gave the taslim, he said, "May Allah have mercy on you, is this the obligatory prayer you performed, or something voluntary you added?" He said, "It is the obligatory prayer, and it is the prayer of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. I have not erred except in something I forgot." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to say: "Do not be harsh upon yourselves, lest harshness be imposed upon you, for a people were harsh upon themselves and harshness was imposed upon them. Those are their remnants in hermitages and monasteries: {monasticism which they invented, We did not prescribe it for them}." Then the next day they went out and said, "Let us ride and look and take heed." He said, "Yes." So they all rode, and they came upon desolate dwellings whose inhabitants had perished, died out, and vanished, fallen upon their own roofs. They said, "Do you recognize these dwellings?" He said, "How well I know them and their inhabitants! These are the people of the dwellings; injustice and envy destroyed them. Indeed envy extinguishes the light of good deeds, and injustice either confirms that or belies it, and the eye commits fornication, and the hand, the foot, the body, and the tongue, and the private part either confirms that or belies it."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Anas ibn Malik reported that the Prophet ﷺ said: "For every prophet there is a monasticism, and the monasticism of this nation is jihad in the way of Allah, Mighty and Majestic."

The hafiz Abu Ya'la related it from Abdullah ibn Muhammad ibn Asma, from Abdullah ibn al-Mubarak, with the wording: "For every nation there is a monasticism, and the monasticism of this nation is jihad in the way of Allah."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, may Allah be pleased with him, reported that a man came to him and said, "Advise me." He said, "You have asked what someone before you asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. I advise you to fear Allah, for that is the head of all things. And hold fast to jihad, for it is the monasticism of Islam. And hold fast to the remembrance of Allah and the recitation of the Qur'an, for it is your spirit in heaven and your remembrance on earth." Ahmad alone related it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ مُنْذُ بَعَثَ نُوحًا، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، لَمْ يُرْسِلْ بَعْدَهُ رَسُولًا وَلَا نَبِيًّا إِلَّا مِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِهِ، وَكَذَلِكَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، خَلِيلُ الرَّحْمَنِ، لَمْ يُنْزِلْ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ كِتَابًا وَلَا أَرْسَلَ رَسُولًا وَلَا أَوْحَى إِلَى بَشَرٍ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ، إِلَّا وَهُوَ مِنْ سُلَالَتِهِ كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَجَعَلْنَا فِي ذُرِّيَّتِهِمَا النُّبُوَّةَ وَالْكِتَابَ﴾ [يَعْنِي] حَتَّى كَانَ آخِرُ أَنْبِيَاءِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ الَّذِي بَشَّرَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ بِمُحَمَّدٍ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِمَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ثُمَّ قَفَّيْنَا عَلَى آثَارِهِمْ بِرُسُلِنَا وَقَفَّيْنَا بِعِيسَى ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ وَآتَيْنَاهُ الإنْجِيلَ﴾

وَهُوَ الْكِتَابُ الَّذِي أَوْحَاهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ ﴿وَجَعَلْنَا فِي قُلُوبِ الَّذِينَ اتَّبَعُوهُ﴾ وَهُمُ الْحَوَارِيُّونَ ﴿رَأْفَةً وَرَحْمَةً﴾ أَيْ: رَأْفَةً وَهِيَ الْخَشْيَةُ ﴿وَرَحْمَةً﴾ بِالْخَلْقِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَرَهْبَانِيَّةً ابْتَدَعُوهَا﴾ أَيِ: ابْتَدَعَتْهَا أُمَّةُ النَّصَارَى ﴿مَا كَتَبْنَاهَا عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: مَا شَرَعْنَاهَا لَهُمْ، وَإِنَّمَا هُمُ الْتَزَمُوهَا مِنْ تِلْقَاءِ أَنْفُسِهِمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِلا ابْتِغَاءَ رِضْوَانِ اللَّهِ﴾ فِيهِ قَوْلَانِ، أَحَدُهُمَا: أَنَّهُمْ قَصَدُوا بِذَلِكَ رِضْوَانَ اللَّهِ، قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ. وَالْآخَرُ: مَا كَتَبْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ ذَلِكَ إِنَّمَا كَتَبْنَا عَلَيْهِمُ ابْتِغَاءَ رِضْوَانِ اللَّهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَمَا رَعَوْهَا حَقَّ رِعَايَتِهَا﴾ أَيْ: فَمَا قَامُوا بِمَا الْتَزَمُوهُ حَقَّ الْقِيَامِ. وَهَذَا ذَمٌّ لَهُمْ مِنْ وَجْهَيْنِ، أَحَدُهُمَا: فِي الِابْتِدَاعِ فِي دِينِ اللَّهِ مَا لَمْ يَأْمُرْ بِهِ اللَّهُ. وَالثَّانِي: فِي عَدَمِ قِيَامِهِمْ بِمَا الْتَزَمُوهُ مِمَّا زَعَمُوا أَنَّهُ قُرْبَةٌ يُقَرِّبُهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ أَبِي حَمْزَةَ أَبُو يَعْقُوبَ الرَّازِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا السِّنْدِيُّ بْنُ عَبْدَوَيْهِ حَدَّثَنَا بُكَيْر بْنُ مَعْرُوفٍ، عَنْ مُقاتِل بْنِ حَيَّان، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عن جده بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: قَالَ لِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَا ابْنَ مَسْعُودٍ". قُلْتُ: لَبَّيْكَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ. قَالَ: "هَلْ عَلِمْتَ أَنَّ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ افْتَرَقُوا عَلَى ثِنْتَيْنِ وَسَبْعِينَ فِرْقَةً؟ لَمْ يَنْجُ مِنْهَا إِلَّا ثَلَاثُ فِرَقٍ، قَامَتْ بَيْنَ الْمُلُوكِ وَالْجَبَابِرَةِ بَعْدَ عِيسَى ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَدَعَتْ إِلَى دِينِ اللَّهِ وَدِينِ عِيسَى ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ، فَقَاتَلَتِ الْجَبَابِرَةَ فقُتلت فَصَبَرَتْ وَنَجَتْ، ثُمَّ قَامَتْ طَائِفَةٌ أُخْرَى لَمْ يَكُنْ لَهَا قُوَّةٌ بِالْقِتَالِ، فَقَامَتْ بَيْنَ الْمُلُوكِ وَالْجَبَابِرَةِ فَدَعَوْا إِلَى دِينِ اللَّهِ وَدِينِ عِيسَى ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ، فَقُتِّلَتْ وَقُطِّعَتْ بِالْمَنَاشِيرِ وَحُرِّقَتْ بِالنِّيرَانِ، فَصَبَرَتْ وَنَجَتْ. ثُمَّ قَامَتْ طَائِفَةٌ أُخْرَى لَمْ يَكُنْ لَهَا قُوَّةٌ بِالْقِتَالِ وَلَمْ تُطِقِ الْقِيَامَ بِالْقِسْطِ، فَلَحِقَتْ بِالْجِبَالِ فَتَعَبَّدَتْ وَتَرَهَّبَتْ، وَهُمُ الَّذِينَ ذَكَرَهُمُ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَرَهْبَانِيَّةً ابْتَدَعُوهَا مَا كَتَبْنَاهَا عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ 

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ بِلَفْظٍ آخَرَ مِنْ طَرِيقٍ أُخْرَى فَقَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا دَاوُدُ بْنُ الْمُحَبَّرِ، حَدَّثَنَا الصَّعِق بْنُ حَزْن، حَدَّثَنَا عُقَيْلٌ الْجَعْدِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ الْهَمْدَانِيِّ، عَنْ سُوَيْد بْنِ غَفَلَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "اخْتَلَفَ مَنْ كَانَ قَبْلنَا عَلَى ثَلَاثٍ وَسَبْعِينَ فِرْقَةً، نَجَا مِنْهُمْ ثَلَاثٌ وَهَلَكَ سَائِرُهُمْ ... " وَذَكَرَ نَحْوَ مَا تَقَدَّمَ، وَفِيهِ: " ﴿فَآتَيْنَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مِنْهُمْ أَجْرَهُمْ﴾ هُمُ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِي وَصَدَّقُونِي ﴿وَكَثِيرٌ مِنْهُمْ فَاسِقُونَ﴾ وَهُمُ الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُونِي وَخَالَفُونِي" 

وَلَا يَقْدَحُ فِي هَذِهِ الْمُتَابَعَةِ لِحَالِ دَاوُدَ بْنِ الْمُحَبَّرِ، فَإِنَّهُ أَحَدُ الْوَضَّاعِينَ لِلْحَدِيثِ، وَلَكِنْ قد أسنده أَبُو يَعْلَى، وَسَنَدُهُ عَنْ شَيْبَانَ بْنِ فَرُّوخ، عَنِ الصَّعِق بْنِ حَزْن، بِهِ مِثْلُ ذَلِكَ فَقَوِيَ الْحَدِيثُ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَأَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ النَّسَائِيُّ-وَاللَّفْظُ لَهُ-: أَخْبَرَنَا الْحُسَيْنُ بْنُ حُرَيْث، حَدَّثَنَا الْفَضْلُ بْنُ مُوسَى، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ السَّائِبِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا قَالَ: كَانَ مُلُوكٌ بَعْدَ عِيسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بَدَّلَتِ التَّوْرَاةَ والإنجيل، فكان منهم مؤمنون يقرؤون التَّوْرَاةَ وَالْإِنْجِيلَ، فَقِيلَ لِمُلُوكِهِمْ: مَا نَجِدُ شَيْئًا أشد من شتم يشتمونا هؤلاء، إنهم يقرؤون: ﴿وَمَنْ لَمْ يَحْكُمْ بِمَا أَنزلَ اللَّهُ فَأُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْكَافِرُونَ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ: ٤٤] ، هَذِهِ الْآيَاتُ، مَعَ مَا يَعِيبُونَنَا بِهِ مِنْ أَعْمَالِنَا فِي قِرَاءَتِهِمْ، فَادْعُهُمْ فليقرؤوا كَمَا نَقْرَأُ، وَلِيُؤْمِنُوا كَمَا آمَنَّا. فَدَعَاهُمْ فَجَمَعَهُمْ وَعَرَضَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْقَتْلَ أَوْ يَتْرُكُوا قِرَاءَةَ التَّوْرَاةِ وَالْإِنْجِيلِ، إِلَّا مَا بَدَّلُوا مِنْهَا، فَقَالُوا: مَا تُرِيدُونَ إِلَى ذَلِكَ؟ دَعُونَا: فَقَالَتْ طَائِفَةٌ مِنْهُمُ: ابْنُوا لَنَا أُسْطُوَانَةً، ثُمَّ ارْفَعُونَا إِلَيْهَا، ثُمَّ أَعْطُونَا شَيْئًا نَرْفَعُ بِهِ طَعَامَنَا وَشَرَابَنَا فَلَا نَرُدُّ عَلَيْكُمْ. وَقَالَتْ طَائِفَةٌ: دَعُونَا نَسِيحُ فِي الْأَرْضِ وَنَهِيمُ وَنَشْرَبُ كَمَا يَشْرَبُ الْوَحْشُ، فَإِنْ قَدَرْتُمْ عَلَيْنَا فِي أَرْضِكُمْ فَاقْتُلُونَا. وَقَالَتْ طَائِفَةٌ: ابْنُوا لَنَا دُورًا فِي الْفَيَافِي، وَنَحْتَفِرُ الْآبَارَ وَنَحْتَرِثُ الْبُقُولَ فَلَا نَرُدُّ عَلَيْكُمْ وَلَا نَمُرُّ بِكُمْ. وَلَيْسَ أَحَدٌ مِنَ الْقَبَائِلِ إِلَّا لَهُ حَمِيمٌ فِيهِمْ، فَفَعَلُوا ذَلِكَ فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَرَهْبَانِيَّةً ابْتَدَعُوهَا مَا كَتَبْنَاهَا عَلَيْهِمْ إِلا ابْتِغَاءَ رِضْوَانِ اللَّهِ فَمَا رَعَوْهَا حَقَّ رِعَايَتِهَا﴾ وَالْآخَرُونَ قَالُوا: نَتَعَبَّدُ كَمَا تَعَبَّدَ فُلَانٌ، وَنَسِيحُ كَمَا سَاحَ فُلَانٌ، وَنَتَّخِذُ دُورًا كَمَا اتَّخَذَ فُلَانٌ، وَهُمْ عَلَى شِرْكِهِمْ لَا عِلْمَ لَهُمْ بِإِيمَانِ الَّذِينَ اقْتَدَوْا بِهِمْ فَلَمَّا بُعث النَّبِيُّ ﷺ وَلَمْ يَبْقَ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا الْقَلِيلُ، انْحَطَّ مِنْهُمْ رَجُلٌ مِنْ صَوْمَعَتِهِ، وَجَاءَ سَائِحٌ مِنْ سِيَاحَتِهِ، وَصَاحِبُ الدَّيْرِ مِنْ دَيْرِهِ، فَآمَنُوا بِهِ وَصَدَّقُوهُ، فَقَالَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَآمِنُوا بِرَسُولِهِ يُؤْتِكُمْ كِفْلَيْنِ مِنْ رَحْمَتِهِ﴾ أَجْرَيْنِ بِإِيمَانِهِمْ بِعِيسَى ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ وَالتَّوْرَاةِ وَالْإِنْجِيلِ، وَبِإِيمَانِهِمْ
